423: 	def _shrinker(self, expr):
424: 		"""
425: 		this modifies an addition, by removing one term at a time
426: 		"""
427: 
428: 		if expr.is_Atom:
429: 			return []
430: 
431: 		ret_exprs = []
432: 		new_exprs = []
433: 
434: 		# handle this being add  (MUL easy by adding 'or expr.is_Mul') [might want to track separately though]
435: 		if expr.is_Add:
436: 			for i,e in enumerate(expr.args):
437: 				cloned_args = list(expr.args)
438: 				del cloned_args[i]
439: 				smaller_add = expr.func(*cloned_args)
440: 				new_exprs.append(smaller_add)
441: 		
442: 		# recursive case
443: 		args_sets = []
444: 		for i,e in enumerate(expr.args):
445: 			if not e.is_Atom:
446: 				ee = self._shrinker(e)
447: 				if len(ee) > 0:
448: 					# We made a removal(s) on an addition down this branch!!
449: 					print(len(expr.args))
450: 					args_map = set(expr.args)
451: 					for vs in ee:
452: 						if self.grow_filter == True and expr.is_Add and vs in args_map:
453: 							continue
454: 						# clone current args
455: 						cloned_args = list(expr.args)
456: 						# replace this term in each
457: 						cloned_args[i] = vs
458: 						# append to the args_sets
459: 						args_sets.append(cloned_args)
460: 
461: 		# finally, create all of the clones at the current level of recursion
462: 		for args in args_sets:
463: 			args = tuple(args)
464: 			tmp = expr.func(*args)
465: 			new_exprs.append(tmp)
466: 
467: 
468: 
469: 		ret_exprs = self._uniquify(new_exprs)
470: 		return ret_exprs
471: 
472: 
473: 
474: 
475: 	def _add_extend(self, expr, limit_sub=False):
476: 		new_exprs = []
477: 		# only worry about non-atoms, cause we extend args
478: 		if not expr.is_Atom:
479: 			args_sets = []
480: 			# however we have 2 cases here (as opposed to _var_sub)
481: 			# 1. extend this expression if it's an Add
482: 			if expr.is_Add:
483: 				sub_terms = self.add_extend_terms
484: 				if limit_sub:
485: 					sub_terms = self.add_extend_lim_terms
486: 				print(len(expr.args))
487: 				args_map = set(expr.args)
488: 				for term in sub_terms:
489: 					# has_match skips extending an add with a term that is already present 
490: 					if self.grow_filter == True and term in args_map:
491: 							continue
492: 					
493: 					cloned_args = list(expr.args)
494: 					cloned_args.append(term)
495: 					args_sets.append(cloned_args)
496: 
497: 			# 2. do the recursion
498: 			for i,e in enumerate(expr.args):
499: 				if not e.is_Atom:
500: 					lim_sub = limit_sub or not (e.is_Add or e.is_Mul)
501: 					ee = self._add_extend(e,limit_sub=lim_sub)
502: 					if len(ee) > 0:
503: 						# We made a substitution(s) on a variable down this branch!!
504: 						print(len(expr.args))
505: 						args_map = set(expr.args)
506: 						for vs in ee:
507: 							if self.grow_filter == True and expr.is_Add and vs in args_map:
508: 								continue
509: 							# clone current args
510: 							cloned_args = list(expr.args)
511: 							# replace this term in each
512: 							cloned_args[i] = vs
513: 							# append to the args_sets
514: 							args_sets.append(cloned_args)
515: 
516: 
517: 			# finally, create all of the clones at the current level of recursion
518: 			for args in args_sets:
519: 				args = tuple(args)
520: 				tmp = expr.func(*args)
521: 				new_exprs.append(tmp)
522: 
523: 		ret_exprs = self._uniquify(new_exprs)
524: 		return ret_exprs
525: 
526: 
527: 
528: 	def _mul_extend(self, expr, limit_sub=False):
529: 		new_exprs = []
530: 		# only worry about non-atoms, cause we extend args
531: 		if not expr.is_Atom:
532: 			args_sets = []
533: 			# however we have 2 cases here (as opposed to _var_sub)
534: 			# 1. extend this expression if it's a Mul
535: 			if expr.is_Mul:
536: 				sub_terms = self.mul_extend_terms
537: 				if limit_sub:
538: 					sub_terms = self.mul_extend_lim_terms
539: 				for term in sub_terms:
540: 					cloned_args = list(expr.args)
541: 					cloned_args.append(term)
542: 					args_sets.append(cloned_args)
543: 
544: 			# 2. do the recursion
545: 			for i,e in enumerate(expr.args):
546: 				if not e.is_Atom:
547: 					lim_sub = limit_sub or not (e.is_Add or e.is_Mul)
548: 					ee = self._mul_extend(e,limit_sub=lim_sub)
549: 					if len(ee) > 0:
550: 						# We made a substitution(s) on a variable down this branch!!
551: 						print(len(expr.args))
552: 						args_map = set(expr.args)
553: 						for vs in ee:
554: 							if self.grow_filter == True and expr.is_Add and vs in args_map:
555: 								continue
556: 							# clone current args
557: 							cloned_args = list(expr.args)
558: 							# replace this term in each
559: 							cloned_args[i] = vs
560: 							# append to the args_sets
561: 							args_sets.append(cloned_args)
562: 
563: 
564: 			# finally, create all of the clones at the current level of recursion
565: 			for args in args_sets:
566: 				args = tuple(args)
567: 				tmp = expr.func(*args)
568: 				new_exprs.append(tmp)
569: 
570: 		
571: 		ret_exprs = self._uniquify(new_exprs)
572: 		return ret_exprs
573: 
574: 
575: 
576: 	def _uniquify(self,exprs):
577: 		## UNIQUIFY THE RESULTS
578: 		pass_set = set()
579: 		for p in exprs:
580: 			s = p.evalf()
581: 			pass_set.add(s)
582: 		return list(pass_set)
583: 
584: 
585: 	def _toggle_plus_C(self, expr):
586: 		if expr.is_Add:
587: 			hasC = False
588: 			for e in expr.args:
589: 				if e == C:
590: 					hasC = True
591: 					break
592: 			if not hasC:
593: 				return expr + C
594: 			else:
595: 				args = [e for e in expr.args if e != C]
596: 				args = tuple(args)
597: 				return expr.func(*args)
598: 		else:
599: 			return sympy.Add(expr, C)

34: 		# default values

41: 		self.peek_npts = 16

56: 		self.fitness_func = "normalized_size_score"

68: 			"func_level": "linear",

70: 			"grow_level": "low",
71: 			"subs_level": "med",

74: 		}

79:

101: 		# self.fitness_calc = fitness_funcs.get_fitness_calc(self.fitness_func)
102: 		print(self.fitness_func)
103:

109: 		if type(self.vars) is sympy.Symbol:
110: 			self.vars = [self.vars]
111:

113: 		if not self.check_config():
114: 			print ("ERROR: config missing values")
115: 			return

123: 		self.peek_nfev = 0 # mul by peek_npts

153: 		for lf in log_files:
154: 			self.logs[lf] = open(self.log_dir + "pge_" + lf + ".log", "w")
155:

157:

160:

162: 		self.hmap = {}

165: 		self.max_heap_size = 50 * self.max_iter
166: 		self.nsga2_list = []
167: 		self.grower = expand.Grower(self.vars, self.usable_funcs, **self.grow_params)
168: 
169: 		# Progressive Evaluation heap
170: 		self.nsga2_peek = []
171: 
172: 		# Progressive Expansion growers
173: 		self.multi_expanders = []
174: 		pprint(self.multi_expander_params)
175: 		for i,p in enumerate(self.multi_expander_params):
176: 			expander = {
177: 			    'pop_count': p.get('pop_count', self.pop_count),
178: 				'nsga2_list': [],
179: 				'grower': expand.Grower(self.vars, expand.map_names_to_funcs(p['usable_funcs']), **(p['grow_params']) )
180: 			}
181: 			self.multi_expanders.append(expander)
182: 
183: 
184: 		# list of all finalized models
185: 		self.final = []
186: 		self.final_paretos = None
187: 
188: 		# Root node for the GRAPH
189: 		r = sympy.Symbol("root")
190: 		self.root_model = model.Model(r)
191: 		R = self.root_model
192: 		R.id = -1
193: 		R.score = 9999999999999.
194: 		R.r2 = -100.
195: 		R.evar = -100.
196: 
197: 		# Relationship Graph
198: 		self.iter_expands = []
199: 		self.iter_expands.append([R])
200: 		self.GRAPH = nx.MultiDiGraph()
201: 		self.GRAPH.add_node(R.id, modl=R)
202: 		s = "{}: node {} ".format(self.curr_iter, R.id)
203: 		print(s, file=self.logs["graph"])
204: 
205: 		self.peek_procs = []
206: 		self.eval_procs = []
207: 		self.alge_procs = []
208: 		self.expd_procs = []
209: 		
210: 		# multiprocessing stuff
211: 		if self.workers > 0:
212: 			self.peek_in_queue = mp.Queue(self.queue_size)
213: 			self.peek_out_queue = mp.Queue(self.queue_size)
214: 			self.peek_procs = [mp.Process(target=parallel.unwrap_self_peek_model_queue, args=(self,) ) for i in range(self.workers)]
215: 
216: 			self.eval_in_queue = mp.Queue(self.queue_size)
217: 			self.eval_out_queue = mp.Queue(self.queue_size)
218: 			self.eval_procs = [mp.Process(target=parallel.unwrap_self_eval_model_queue, args=(self,) ) for i in range(self.workers)]
219: 
220: 			self.alge_in_queue = mp.Queue(self.queue_size)
221: 			self.alge_out_queue = mp.Queue(self.queue_size)
222: 			self.alge_procs = [mp.Process(target=parallel.unwrap_self_alge_model_queue, args=(self,) ) for i in range(self.workers)]
223: 
224: 			self.expd_in_queue = mp.Queue(self.queue_size)
225: 			self.expd_out_queue = mp.Queue(self.queue_size)
226: 			self.expd_procs = [mp.Process(target=parallel.unwrap_self_expd_model_queue, args=(self,) ) for i in range(self.workers)]
227: 
228: 
229: 		# possibly connect to remote host via websocket
230: 		if self.remote_eval == True:
231: 			self.ws = create_connection(self.remote_host)
232: 			data = {
233: 				'Kind': "WorkerCnt",
234: 				'Payload': self.remote_cores
235: 			}
236: 
237: 			msg = json.dumps(data)
238: 
239: 			print("sending WorkerCnt: ")
240: 			self.ws.send(msg)
241: 			ok = self.ws.recv()
242: 			print("WorkerCnt ret: ", ok)
243:

250: 	def check_config(self):
251: 		"""
252: 			This function checks the correctness of the PGE configuration.
253: 			It is not quite complete at the time of this writing
254: 		"""
255: 		if self.search_vars == None \
256: 		or self.usable_vars == None:
257: 			return False
258: 
259: 		complexities = ["low","med","high"]
260: 		if self.init_level not in complexities \
261: 		or self.grow_level not in complexities:
262: 			return False
263: 
264: 
265: 		return True
266: 
267: 	def assign_iter_id(self, expr_list):
268: 		for e in expr_list:
269: 			e.iter_id = self.curr_iter
270: 
271: 
272: 	# sklearn estimator interface functions
273: 	def fit(self, X_train,Y_train):
274: 
275: 		start = time.time()
276: 		self.start_time = start
277: 
278: 		self.set_data(X_train,Y_train) # *** see note below
279: 		self.preloop()
280: 		self.loop(self.max_iter)
281: 		self.finalize()
282: 
283: 		end = time.time()
284: 
285: 		runtime = '     {:14.4f} seconds'.format(end - start)
286: 		print("TOTAL RUN TIME:", runtime)
287: 
288: 		### Sklearn doesn't want us to store this data
289: 		### But we want to for checkpointing and continuation
290: 		### This may require a finalization function
291: 		###   as we are finalizing at the end of loop right now
292: 		###   either way, we want sklean interface, with curr finalization
293: 		###   while still checkpointing, just need more storage and temps
294: 
295: 
296: 	def set_data(self, X_train, Y_train):
297: 		# set training data 
298: 		self.X_train = X_train
299: 		self.Y_train = Y_train
300: 		self.eval_npts = len(self.Y_train)
301: 
302: 		# set peeking data
303: 		pos = numpy.random.randint(0,self.eval_npts, self.peek_npts)
304: 		self.X_peek = self.X_train[:,pos]
305: 		self.Y_peek = self.Y_train[pos]
306: 
307: 		print ("train.shape:", self.X_train.shape, self.Y_train.shape)
308: 		print ("train.T.shape:", self.X_train.T.shape)
309: 		print ("peekn.shape:", self.X_peek.shape, self.Y_peek.shape)
310: 		print ("\n\n")
311: 
312: 		if self.remote_eval == True:
313: 			data = {
314: 				'Kind': "InputPeek",
315: 				'Payload': self.X_peek.T.tolist()
316: 			}
317: 
318: 			msg = json.dumps(data)
319: 
320: 			print("sending InputPeek: ")
321: 			self.ws.send(msg)
322: 			ok = self.ws.recv()
323: 			print("InputPeek ret: ", ok)
324: 
325: 			data = {
326: 				'Kind': "OutputPeek",
327: 				'Payload': self.Y_peek.tolist()
328: 			}
329: 
330: 			msg = json.dumps(data)
331: 
332: 			print("sending OutputPeek: ")
333: 			self.ws.send(msg)
334: 			ok = self.ws.recv()
335: 			print("OutputPeek ret: ", ok)
336: 
337: 
338: 			data = {
339: 				'Kind': "InputData",
340: 				'Payload': self.X_train.T.tolist()
341: 			}
342: 
343: 			msg = json.dumps(data)
344: 
345: 			print("sending InputData: ")
346: 			self.ws.send(msg)
347: 			ok = self.ws.recv()
348: 			print("InputData ret: ", ok)
349: 
350: 			data = {
351: 				'Kind': "OutputData",
352: 				'Payload': self.Y_train.tolist()
353: 			}
354: 
355: 			msg = json.dumps(data)
356: 
357: 			print("sending OutputData: ")
358: 			self.ws.send(msg)
359: 			ok = self.ws.recv()
360: 			print("OutputData ret: ", ok)
361: 
362: 
363: 
364: 	def preloop(self):
365: 		# preloop setup (generates,evals,queues first models)
366: 		print ("Preloop setup")
367: 
368: 		if self.workers > 0:
369: 			for proc in self.peek_procs:
370: 				proc.start()
371: 			for proc in self.eval_procs:
372: 				proc.start()
373: 			for proc in self.alge_procs:
374: 				proc.start()
375: 			for proc in self.expd_procs:
376: 				proc.start()
377: 
378: 		L = None
379: 		if self.log_details:
380: 			L = self.logs
381: 		T = None
382: 		if self.print_timing:
383: 			T = timewith()
384: 
385: 		def pfunc(msg, iarg, numto=0, lognames=["stdout"], final=False):
386: 			if T:
387: 				s = "  {:3d} {:24s}| {:4d} ".format(self.curr_iter, msg, iarg)
388: 				if numto == 0:
389: 					s += "        "
390: 				else:
391: 					s += "-> {:4d} ".format(numto)
392: 				if final:
393: 					s += T.finalize()
394: 					s += '      {:10.4f} total runtime'.format(self.curr_time - self.start_time)
395: 				else:
396: 					s += T.checkpoint(iarg)
397: 
398: 				if len(lognames) == 0:
399: 					return s
400: 				elif L is not None:
401: 					for logname in lognames:
402: 						print(s, file=L[logname])
403: 
404: 
405: 		# create first models
406: 		first_exprs = self.multi_expanders[0]['grower'].first_exprs()
407: 		self.assign_iter_id(first_exprs)
408: 		pfunc("create first exprs", len(first_exprs), lognames=["stdout","main"])
409: 
410: 		# filter and memoize first_exprs models
411: 		to_memo = self.filter_models(first_exprs)
412: 		pfunc("first => filtered", len(first_exprs), numto=len(to_memo), lognames=["stdout","main"])
413: 
414: 		to_alge = []
415: 		if self.algebra_methods is not None and len(self.algebra_methods) > 0:
416: 			to_alge = self.memoize_models(to_memo)
417: 			pfunc("memoize => algebra", len(to_memo), numto=len(to_alge), lognames=["stdout","main"])
418: 
419: 			# algebra the models which made it through
420: 			algebrad = self.algebra_models(to_alge)
421: 			self.assign_iter_id(algebrad)
422: 			pfunc("algebra => result models", len(to_alge), numto=len(algebrad), lognames=["stdout","main"])
423: 
424: 			# filter and memoize the algebrad models
425: 			to_memo = self.filter_models(algebrad)
426: 			pfunc("algebrad => filtered", len(algebrad), numto=len(to_memo), lognames=["stdout","main"])
427: 
428: 		to_peek = self.memoize_models(to_memo)
429: 		pfunc("memoized => fitting", len(to_memo), numto=len(to_peek), lognames=["stdout","main"])
430: 
431: 		# pass along the unique expressions, plus the algebrad offspring unique
432: 		to_peek = to_alge + to_peek
433: 		pfunc("total for fitting", len(to_peek), lognames=["stdout","main"])
434: 
435: 
436: 		to_eval = []
437: 		if self.peek_npts == 0:
438: 			to_eval = to_peek
439: 		else:
440: 			self.eval_models(to_peek, peek=True)
441: 			pfunc("peeking", len(to_peek), lognames=["stdout","main"])
442: 
443: 			self.peek_push_models(to_peek)
444: 			pfunc("peek pushing", len(to_peek), lognames=["stdout","main"])
445: 
446: 			fromlen = len(self.nsga2_peek)
447: 			to_eval = self.peek_pop() + self.peek_pop() # twice the first time
448: 			pfunc("peek popping", fromlen, numto=len(to_eval), lognames=["stdout","main"])
449: 
450: 
451: 		self.eval_models(to_eval)
452: 		pfunc("evaling", len(to_eval), lognames=["stdout","main"])
453: 
454: 		# after fully eval'd, push to final_paretos
455: 		self.final_push(to_eval)
456: 
457: 		# self.eval_push_models(to_eval)
458: 		self.heap_push(self.multi_expanders[0]['nsga2_list'], to_eval)
459: 		pfunc("eval pushing", len(to_eval), lognames=["stdout","main"])
460: 
461: 		self.curr_time = time.time()
462: 		pfunc("total preloop time", -1, final=True, lognames=["stdout","main"])
463: 
464: 		self.print_best(16)
465: 
466: 		if self.log_details:
467: 			for name, file_obj in self.logs.items():
468: 				file_obj.flush()
469: 
470: 
471: 
472: 	def loop(self, iterations):
473: 		# main loop for # iterations
474: 		for I in range(iterations):
475: 			print ("\n\nITER: ", I)
476: 			self.curr_iter = I
477: 		
478: 			L = None
479: 			if self.log_details:
480: 				L = self.logs
481: 			T = None
482: 			if self.print_timing:
483: 				T = timewith()
484: 
485: 			def pfunc(msg, iarg, numto=0, lognames=["stdout"], final=False):
486: 				if T:
487: 					s = "  {:3d} {:24s}| {:4d} ".format(self.curr_iter, msg, iarg)
488: 					if numto == 0:
489: 						s += "        "
490: 					else:
491: 						s += "-> {:4d} ".format(numto)
492: 					if final:
493: 						s += T.finalize()
494: 						s += '      {:10.4f} total runtime'.format(self.curr_time - self.start_time)
495: 					else:
496: 						s += T.checkpoint(iarg)
497: 
498: 					if len(lognames) == 0:
499: 						return s
500: 					else:
501: 						for logname in lognames:
502: 							print(s, file=L[logname])
503: 
504: 
505: 			# Multi expand and grow
506: 			curr = []
507: 			prev = []
508: 			popd = []
509: 			expanded = []
510: 			for i,_ in enumerate(self.multi_expanders):
511: 				nsga2_list = self.multi_expanders[i]['nsga2_list']
512: 				pop_count = self.multi_expanders[i]['pop_count']
513: 				grower = self.multi_expanders[i]['grower']
514: 
515: 				if len(prev) > 0:
516: 					self.heap_push(nsga2_list, prev)
517: 
518: 				fromlen = len(nsga2_list)
519: 				curr, nsga2_list = self.heap_pop(nsga2_list, pop_count, self.fitness_calc)
520: 				popd.extend(curr)
521: 				pfunc("heap " + str(i) + " popping", fromlen, numto=len(curr), lognames=["stdout","main"])
522: 
523: 				expand_tmp = self.expand_models(curr, grower)
524: 				pfunc("popped => expanded", len(curr), numto=len(expand_tmp), lognames=["stdout","main"])
525: 				expanded.extend(expand_tmp)
526: 
527: 				self.multi_expanders[i]['nsga2_list'] = nsga2_list
528: 				prev = curr
529: 
530: 
531: 			self.assign_iter_id(expanded)
532: 			# pfunc("popped => expanded", len(popd), numto=len(expanded), lognames=["stdout","main"])
533: 
534: 
535: 			# filter and memoize expanded models
536: 			to_memo = self.filter_models(expanded)			
537: 			pfunc("expanded => filtered", len(expanded), numto=len(to_memo), lognames=["stdout","main"])
538: 
539: 			to_alge = []
540: 			if self.algebra_methods is not None and len(self.algebra_methods) > 0:
541: 				to_alge = self.memoize_models(to_memo)
542: 				pfunc("memoize => algebra", len(to_memo), numto=len(to_alge), lognames=["stdout","main"])
543: 
544: 				# algebra the models which made it through
545: 				algebrad = self.algebra_models(to_alge)
546: 				self.assign_iter_id(algebrad)
547: 				pfunc("algebra => result models", len(to_alge), numto=len(algebrad), lognames=["stdout","main"])
548: 
549: 				# filter and memoize the algebrad models
550: 				to_memo = self.filter_models(algebrad)
551: 				pfunc("algebrad => filtered", len(algebrad), numto=len(to_memo), lognames=["stdout","main"])
552: 
553: 			to_peek = self.memoize_models(to_memo)
554: 			pfunc("memoized => fitting", len(to_memo), numto=len(to_peek), lognames=["stdout","main"])
555: 
556: 			# pass along the unique expressions, plus the algebrad offspring unique
557: 			to_peek = to_alge + to_peek
558: 			pfunc("total for fitting", len(to_peek), lognames=["stdout","main"])
559: 
560: 
561: 			to_eval = []
562: 			if self.peek_npts == 0:
563: 				to_eval = to_peek
564: 			else:
565: 				# peek evaluate the unique models
566: 				self.eval_models(to_peek, peek=True)
567: 				pfunc("peeking", len(to_peek), lognames=["stdout","main"])
568: 
569: 				# push the peek'd models
570: 				self.peek_push_models(to_peek)
571: 				pfunc("peek pushing", len(to_peek), lognames=["stdout","main"])
572: 
573: 				# pop some models for full evaluation
574: 				fromlen = len(self.nsga2_peek)
575: 				to_eval = self.peek_pop()
576: 				pfunc("peek popping", fromlen, numto=len(to_eval), lognames=["stdout","main"])
577: 
578: 			# fully fit and evaluate these models
579: 			self.eval_models(to_eval)
580: 			pfunc("evaling", len(to_eval), lognames=["stdout","main"])
581: 
582: 			# after fully eval'd, push to final_paretos
583: 			self.final_push(to_eval)
584: 
585: 			# push fully fit models into the queue for expansion candidacy
586: 			# self.eval_push_models(to_eval)
587: 			self.heap_push(self.multi_expanders[0]['nsga2_list'], to_eval)
588: 			pfunc("eval pushing", len(to_eval), lognames=["stdout","main"])
589: 
590: 			self.curr_time = time.time()
591: 			pfunc("total loop time", I, final=True, lognames=["stdout","main"])
592: 			self.print_best(32)
593: 
594: 			s = "{:3d} {:.4f} {} {}   {} {} {} {} {}   {} {} {} {}   {} {} {} {}".format(
595: 					self.curr_iter,
596: 					self.curr_time - self.start_time,
597: 					self.peekd_models, 
598: 					self.evald_models,
599: 
600: 					self.peek_nfev, 
601: 					self.peek_nfev * self.peek_npts,
602: 					self.eval_nfev, 
603: 					self.eval_nfev * self.eval_npts,
604: 					self.peek_nfev * self.peek_npts + self.eval_nfev * self.eval_npts,
605: 
606: 					self.best_size,
607: 					self.best_err,
608: 					self.best_r2,
609: 					self.best_vari,
610: 
611: 					self.ave_size,
612: 					self.ave_err,
613: 					self.ave_r2,
614: 					self.ave_vari
615: 
616: 				)
617: 			print(s, file=self.logs["errs"])
618: 
619: 			if self.log_details:
620: 				for name, file_obj in self.logs.items():
621: 					file_obj.flush()
622: 
623: 
624: 
625: 	def print_best(self, count, file=sys.stdout):
626: 		print ("Best " + str(count) + " of " + str(len(self.final)), file=file)
627: 		# self.fitness_calc(self.final)
628: 		models = self.heap_select(self.final, count, self.fitness_calc)
629: 		best = selection.sortLogNondominated(models, count)
630: 		print (best[0][0].print_long_columns(), file=file)
631: 		print ("-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------", file=file)
632: 		cnt = 0
633: 		self.best_size = 0
634: 		self.best_err = 10000000000
635: 		self.best_r2 = 0
636: 		self.best_vari = 0
637: 		self.ave_size = 0
638: 		self.ave_err = 0
639: 		self.ave_r2 = 0
640: 		self.ave_vari = 0
641: 
642: 		for front in best:
643: 			for m in front:
644: 				if cnt >= count:
645: 					break
646: 				cnt += 1
647: 				print ("  ", m.print_long(), file=file)
648: 
649: 				if m.score < self.best_err:
650: 					self.best_size = m.size()
651: 					self.best_err = m.score
652: 					self.best_r2 = m.r2
653: 					self.best_vari = m.evar
654: 				self.ave_size += m.size()
655: 				self.ave_err += m.score
656: 				self.ave_r2 += m.r2
657: 				self.ave_vari += m.evar
658: 
659: 			print ("", file=file)
660: 			if cnt >= count:
661: 				break
662: 
663: 		self.ave_size /= float(count)
664: 		self.ave_err /= float(count)
665: 		self.ave_r2 /= float(count)
666: 		self.ave_vari /= float(count)
667: 
668: 		print ("-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------", file=file)
669: 
670: 
671: 	def print_final_models(self, model_list, count, file=sys.stdout):
672: 		print (model_list[0][0].print_csv_columns(), file=file)
673: 
674: 		cnt = 0
675: 		for front in model_list:
676: 			for m in front:
677: 				if cnt >= count:
678: 					return
679: 				cnt += 1
680: 				print (m.print_csv(), file=file)
681: 
682: 
683: 	def finalize(self, nfronts=4):
684: 		# finalization
685: 		print ("\n\nFinalizing\n\n")
686: 
687: 		# pull all non-expanded models in queue out and push into final
688: 		# could also use spea2_list here, they should have same contents
689: 		final = self.final + self.nsga2_list 
690: 
691: 		# generate final pareto fronts
692: 		self.fitness_calc(final)
693: 		final_list = selection.sortLogNondominated(final, len(final))
694: 
695: 		self.print_final_models(final_list, 128, self.logs["final"])
696: 
697: 		# print first 4 pareto fronts
698: 		print ("Final Results")
699: 		print (final_list[0][0].print_columns())
700: 		print ("-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------")
701: 		for front in final_list[:nfronts]:
702: 			for m in front:
703: 				print ("  ", m)
704: 			print ("")
705: 
706: 		print ("\n")
707: 		print ("num peekd models:  ", self.peekd_models)
708: 		print ("num evald models:  ", self.evald_models)
709: 		print ("num peek evals:  ", self.peek_nfev, self.peek_nfev * self.peek_npts)
710: 		print ("num eval evals:  ", self.eval_nfev, self.eval_nfev * self.eval_npts)
711: 		print ("num total evals: ", self.peek_nfev * self.peek_npts + self.eval_nfev * self.eval_npts)
712: 		
713: 		# print ("\n\n", nx.info(self.GRAPH), "\n\n")
714: 
715: 		# handle issue with extra stray node with parent_id == -2 (at end of nodes list)
716: 		# del_n = []
717: 		# for n in nx.nodes_iter(self.GRAPH):
718: 		# 	modl = self.memoizer.get_by_id(n)
719: 		# 	if modl.score is None:
720: 		# 		del_n.append(n)
721: 		# for n in del_n:
722: 		# 	self.GRAPH.remove_node(n)
723: 
724: 
725: 		if self.workers > 0:
726: 			print ("\n\nstopping workers")
727: 			for proc in self.peek_procs:
728: 				self.peek_in_queue.put(None)
729: 			for proc in self.eval_procs:
730: 				self.eval_in_queue.put(None)
731: 			for proc in self.alge_procs:
732: 				self.alge_in_queue.put(None)
733: 			for proc in self.expd_procs:
734: 				self.expd_in_queue.put(None)
735: 
736: 			for proc in self.peek_procs:
737: 				proc.join()
738: 			for proc in self.eval_procs:
739: 				proc.join()
740: 			for proc in self.alge_procs:
741: 				proc.join()
742: 			for proc in self.expd_procs:
743: 				proc.join()
744: 
745: 		if self.remote_eval == True:
746: 			self.ws.close()
747: 
748: 
749: 		print ("\n\ndone\n\n")
750: 
751: 		if self.log_details:
752: 			for name, file_obj in self.logs.items():
753: 				if file_obj is not sys.stdout:
754: 					file_obj.close()
755: 					
756: 	def get_final_paretos(self):
757: 		# pull all non-expanded models in queue out and push into final
758: 		# could also use spea2_list here, they should have same contents
759: 		final = self.final + self.nsga2_list 
760: 
761: 		# generate final pareto fronts
762: 		self.fitness_calc(final)
763: 		final_list = selection.sortLogNondominated(final, len(final))
764: 		return final_list

766: 	def filter_models(self, models):
767: 		passed = filters.filter_models(models, filters.default_filters)
768: 		return passed

771: 	def memoize_models(self, models, progress=False):
772: 		# print ("  MEMOIZING:", len(models))
773: 		L = len(models)
774: 		ppp = L / 20
775: 		PPP = ppp
776: 		if progress:
777: 			which = "memo'n"
778: 			print("     ", which, L, ppp, "  ", end="", flush=True)
779: 			
780: 		for i,m in enumerate(models):
781: 			if progress and i >= PPP:
782: 				print('.',end="",flush=True)
783: 				PPP += ppp
784: 
785: 
786: 
787: 			did_ins = False
788: 			r = self.hmap.get(m.orig,None)
789: 			if r is None:
790: 				did_ins = True
791: 				m.id = len(self.models)
792: 				self.models.append(m)
793: 				self.hmap[m.orig] = m
794: 
795: 			# found, f_modl = self.memoizer.lookup(m)
796: 			# print(i, found, m.id, m.orig)
797: 			# if found:
798: 			# 	# NEED TO REVERSE SOME EDGES HERE FOR SHRINKING
799: 			# 	self.GRAPH.add_edge(m.parent_id, f_modl.id, relation=m.gen_relation)
800: 			# 	s = "{}: EDGE {} -> {} r {}".format(self.curr_iter, m.parent_id, f_modl.id, m.gen_relation)
801: 			# 	print(s, file=self.logs["graph"])
802: 
803: 			# did_ins = self.memoizer.insert(m)
804: 			if did_ins:
805: 				m.memoized = True
806: 				# unique.append(m)
807: 				# add node and edge
808: 				# self.GRAPH.add_node(m.id, modl=m)				
809: 				# s = "{}: node {} ".format(self.curr_iter, m.id)
810: 				# print(s, file=self.logs["graph"])
811: 				# print(s, m.orig, file=self.logs["nodes"])
812: 
813: 				# # NEED TO REVERSE SOME EDGES HERE FOR SHRINKING
814: 				# self.GRAPH.add_edge(m.parent_id, m.id, relation=m.gen_relation)
815: 				# s = "{}: edge {} -> {} r {}".format(self.curr_iter, m.parent_id, m.id, m.gen_relation)
816: 				# print(s, file=self.logs["graph"])
817: 
818: 		# print ("  UNIQUE:", len(unique),"/",len(models))
819: 		if progress:
820: 			print()
821: 
822: 		unique = [m for m in models if m.memoized]
823: 		return unique
824: 
825: 	def expand_models(self, models, grower):
826: 		if self.workers > 0:
827: 			return self.expand_models_multiprocess(models, grower)
828: 		else:
829: 			# print ("  algebra:", len(models))
830: 			return self.grow_models(models, grower)
831: 
832: 	def grow_models(self, models, grower):
833: 		expanded = []
834: 		for p in models:
835: 			modls = grower.grow(p)
836: 			expanded.extend(modls)
837: 		return expanded
838: 
839: 
840: 	def expand_models_multiprocess(self, models, grower):
841: 		# print ("  multi algebra:", len(models))
842: 		expanded = []
843: 		
844: 		for i,m in enumerate(models):
845: 			try:
846: 				self.expd_in_queue.put( (i,m, grower) )
847: 			except Exception as e:
848: 				print ("expd send error!", e, "\n  ", i, m.expr)
849: 				break
850: 
851: 		
852: 		for i in range(len(models)):
853: 			try:
854: 				ret = self.expd_out_queue.get()
855: 			except Exception as e:
856: 				print ("expd recv error!", e, "\n  ", i)
857: 				break
858: 
859: 			pos = ret[0]
860: 			err = ret[1]
861: 			expd = ret[2]
862: 
863: 			print("Expanded: ", pos, len(expd))
864: 
865: 			if err is not None:
866: 				if err == "same":
867: 					continue
868: 				else:
869: 					print ("Error:", err)
870: 			else:
871: 				expanded.extend(expd)
872: 
873: 		return expanded
874: 
875: 	def algebra_models(self, models):
876: 		if self.workers > 0:
877: 			return self.algebra_models_multiprocess(models)
878: 		else:
879: 			# print ("  algebra:", len(models))
880: 			alges = []
881: 			for modl in models:
882: 				for meth in self.algebra_methods:
883: 					manipd, err = algebra.manip_model(modl,meth)
884: 					if err is not None:
885: 						if err == "same":
886: 							continue
887: 						else:
888: 							print ("Error:", err)
889: 					else:
890: 						# print (modl.expr, "==", meth, "==>", manipd.expr, manipd.xs, manipd.cs)
891: 						manipd.parent_id = modl.id
892: 						manipd.gen_relation = meth
893: 						alges.append(manipd)
894: 				modl.algebrad = True
895: 			return alges
896: 
897: 	def algebra_models_multiprocess(self, models):
898: 		# print ("  multi algebra:", len(models))
899: 		alges = []
900: 		
901: 		for i,m in enumerate(models):
902: 			for meth in self.algebra_methods:
903: 				try:
904: 					self.alge_in_queue.put( (i,m, meth) )
905: 				except Exception as e:
906: 					print ("alge send error!", e, "\n  ", i, m.expr)
907: 					break
908: 			m.algebrad = True
909: 
910: 		
911: 		for i in range(len(models) * 2):
912: 			try:
913: 				ret = self.alge_out_queue.get()
914: 			except Exception as e:
915: 				print ("alge recv error!", e, "\n  ", i)
916: 				break
917: 
918: 			pos = ret[0]
919: 			err = ret[1]
920: 			meth = ret[2]
921: 			manipd = ret[3]
922: 			modl = models[ret[0]]
923: 
924: 			if err is not None:
925: 				if err == "same":
926: 					continue
927: 				else:
928: 					print ("Error:", err)
929: 			else:
930: 				manipd.parent_id = modl.id
931: 				manipd.gen_relation = meth
932: 				alges.append(manipd)
933: 
934: 		return alges
935: 
936: 
937: 	def peek_push_models(self, models):
938: 
939: 		ms = [m for m in models if m is not None and m.errored is False and m.score is not None]
940: 		
941: 		self.nsga2_peek.extend(ms)
942: 
943: 		for m in ms:
944: 			m.peek_queued = True
945: 		return ms
946: 
947: 	def peek_pop(self):
948: 		
949: 		popped, heap = self.heap_pop(self.nsga2_peek,self.peek_count,self.fitness_calc)
950: 
951: 		self.fitness_calc(self.nsga2_peek)
952: 
953: 		for p in popped:
954: 			p.peek_popped = True
955: 
956: 		self.nsga2_peek = heap
957: 		# self.nsga2_peek = [m for m in heap if not m.peek_popped]
958: 
959: 		return popped
960: 
961: 
962: 	def final_push(self,models):
963: 		ms = [m for m in models if m is not None and m.errored is False and m.score is not None]
964: 		for p in ms:			
965: 			self.final.append(p)
966: 			p.finalized = True
967: 
968: 	def heap_push(self,heap_list, models):
969: 		ms = [m for m in models if m is not None and m.errored is False and m.score is not None]
970: 		heap_list.extend(ms)
971: 		return ms, heap_list
972: 
973: 	def heap_pop(self, heap_list, pop_count, fitness_calc):
974: 		fitness_calc(heap_list)
975: 
976: 		if self.use_nsga2:
977: 			popped = selection.selNSGA2(heap_list, pop_count, nd='log')
978: 		else:
979: 			popped = selection.sortLogNondominated(heap_list, pop_count, True)
980: 			popped = [ p for plist in popped for p in plist]
981: 			# print("popped", popped)
982: 
983: 		heap_list = [m for m in heap_list if not m in popped]
984: 
985: 		if self.max_heap_size > 0 and len(heap_list) > self.max_heap_size:
986: 			heap_list = heap_list[:self.max_heap_size]
987: 
988: 
989: 		return popped, heap_list
990: 
991: 	def heap_select(self, heap_list, pop_count, fitness_calc):
992: 		fitness_calc(heap_list)
993: 		if self.use_nsga2:
994: 			selected = selection.selNSGA2(heap_list, pop_count, nd='log')
995: 		else:
996: 			selected = selection.sortLogNondominated(heap_list, pop_count, True)
997: 			selected = [ s for slist in selected for s in slist]
998: 			# print("selected", selected)
999: 
1000: 		return selected
1001: 
1002: 
1003: 	def eval_models(self, models, peek=False, progress=True):
1004: 
1005: 		if self.remote_eval == True:
1006: 			self.eval_models_remote(models,peek,progress)
1007: 		else:
1008: 			self.eval_models_local(models,peek,progress)
1009: 
1010: 
1011: 	def eval_models_local(self, models, peek=False, progress=False):
1012: 
1013: 		if self.workers > 0:
1014: 			self.eval_models_multiprocess(models, peek, progress)
1015: 
1016: 		else:
1017: 			L = len(models)
1018: 			ppp = L / 10
1019: 			PPP = ppp
1020: 			if progress:
1021: 				which = "peek'n" if peek else "eval'n"
1022: 				print("     ", which, L, ppp, "  ", end="", flush=True)
1023: 			
1024: 			for i,modl in enumerate(models):
1025: 				if progress and i >= PPP:
1026: 					print('.',end="",flush=True)
1027: 					PPP += ppp
1028: 				passed = evaluate.eval_model(modl, self.vars, self.X_train, self.Y_train, self.err_method)
1029: 				if not passed or modl.error is not None:
1030: 					info = "{:5d}  ERROR     ".format(modl.id)
1031: 					print(info, modl.expr, modl.jac, file=self.logs["evals"])
1032: 
1033: 				else:
1034: 
1035: 					if peek:
1036: 						modl.peek_score  = modl.score
1037: 						modl.peek_r2     = modl.r2
1038: 						modl.peek_evar   = modl.evar
1039: 						modl.peek_aic    = modl.aic
1040: 						modl.peek_bic    = modl.bic
1041: 						modl.peek_chisqr = modl.chisqr
1042: 						modl.peek_redchi = modl.redchi
1043: 
1044: 						modl.peek_nfev = dat['nfev']
1045: 						self.peek_nfev += modl.peek_nfev
1046: 						self.peekd_models += 1
1047: 					
1048: 						modl.peeked = True
1049: 
1050: 					else:
1051: 						modl.eval_nfev += dat['nfev']
1052: 						self.eval_nfev += modl.eval_nfev
1053: 						self.evald_models += 1
1054: 		
1055: 						modl.evaluated = True
1056: 
1057: 					# info = "{:5d}  {:5d}     ".format(modl.id, modl.eval_nfev)
1058: 					# print(info, modl.expr, modl.jac, file=self.logs["evals"])
1059: 			
1060: 					if modl.parent_id >= 0:
1061: 						parent = self.models[modl.parent_id]
1062: 						modl.improve_score = parent.score - modl.score
1063: 						modl.improve_r2 = modl.r2 - parent.r2
1064: 						modl.improve_evar = modl.evar - parent.evar
1065: 						modl.improve_aic = parent.aic - modl.aic
1066: 						modl.improve_bic = parent.bic - modl.bic
1067: 						modl.improve_redchi = parent.redchi - modl.redchi
1068: 					else:
1069: 						# should probaly normalized this across the initial population and permenately set
1070: 						modl.improve_score  = -0.000001 * modl.score
1071: 						modl.improve_r2     = -0.000001 * modl.r2
1072: 						modl.improve_evar   = -0.000001 * modl.evar
1073: 						modl.improve_aic    = -0.000001 * modl.aic
1074: 						modl.improve_bic    = -0.000001 * modl.bic
1075: 						modl.improve_redchi = -0.000001 * modl.redchi
1076: 
1077: 		if progress:
1078: 			print("")
1079: 
1080: 
1081: 	def eval_models_multiprocess(self, models, peek=False, progress=False):
1082: 
1083: 		for i,m in enumerate(models):
1084: 			pkg = (i,m)
1085: 			self.eval_in_queue.put( pkg )
1086: 
1087: 		L = len(models)
1088: 		ppp = L / 10
1089: 		PPP = ppp
1090: 		if progress:
1091: 			which = "peek'n" if peek else "eval'n"
1092: 			print("     ", which, L, ppp, "  ", end="", flush=True)
1093: 
1094: 		for i in range(L):
1095: 			if progress and i >= PPP:
1096: 				print('.',end="",flush=True)
1097: 				PPP += ppp
1098: 
1099: 			ret = self.eval_out_queue.get()
1100: 			pos = ret[0]
1101: 			err = ret[1]
1102: 			dat = ret[2]
1103: 
1104: 			try:
1105: 				modl = models[pos]
1106: 			except Exception as e:
1107: 				print ("POS ERROR: ", pos, len(models), e, ret)
1108: 				continue
1109: 
1110: 			if err is not None:
1111: 				# print("ERROR IS NOT NONE", err)
1112: 				modl.error = err
1113: 				modl.exception = dat
1114: 				modl.errored = True
1115: 			else:
1116: 				modl.score = dat['score']
1117: 				modl.r2 = dat['r2']
1118: 				modl.evar = dat['evar']

<content>
1: # pge-jax — Agent Instructions
2: 
3: ## Project Structure
4: 
5: ```
6: pge-jax/
7: ├── pge_jax/          # Package source
8: │   ├── __init__.py   # Public API — add new exports here
9: │   ├── model.py      # JAXModel: sympy → JAX evaluation wrapper
10: │   ├── optimize.py   # LM and BFGS optimizers
11: │   ├── metrics.py    # JAX-native regression metrics
12: │   └── evaluate.py   # High-level fit/predict/evaluate pipeline
13: ├── tests/            # pytest test suite
14: ├── pyproject.toml    # Build config, deps, tool settings
15: ├── README.md         # User-facing documentation
16: └── AGENTS.md         # This file
17: ```
18: 
19: ## Running the Code
20: 
21: ```bash
22: # Enter the venv (created during setup)
23: source .venv/bin/activate
24: 
25: # Run all tests
26: python -m pytest tests/ -v
27: 
28: # Run a single test file
29: python -m pytest tests/test_model.py -v
30: 
31: # Run a single test
32: python -m pytest tests/test_model.py::TestJAXModel::test_linear_model_basic -v
33: 
34: # Lint
35: ruff check pge_jax/ tests/
36: 
37: # Format
38: ruff format pge_jax/ tests/
39: 
40: # Type check
41: mypy pge_jax/
42: ```
43: 
44: ## Coding Conventions
45: 
46: - **Python 3.11+** — use modern syntax: `X | Y` unions, `match`/`case`, `typing.Self`
47: - **120-char line limit** — configured in `pyproject.toml`
48: - **Docstrings** — Google style (parameters, returns, raises sections)
49: - **Imports** — standard library first, then third-party, then local (`pge_jax.*`), alphabetized within groups
50: - **No bare `import jax`** — always `import jax.numpy as jnp` for array ops
51: - **Type hints** — preferred on all public functions and class attributes
52: - **No print statements** in library code — use logging or return values
53: 
54: ## Core Architecture
55: 
56: ### The Evaluation Pipeline
57: 
58: The key abstraction is `JAXModel` (model.py). It wraps a sympy expression and provides JAX-compatible evaluation:
59: 
60: 1. **Symbol extraction** — `_extract_coeffs_and_vars()` splits `expr.free_symbols` into coefficients (`C_*`) and variables. Sorted by string name for determinism.
61: 
62: 2. **JAX function construction** — `sympy.lambdify(all_syms, expr, modules="jax")` creates a callable. The wrapper unpacks the coefficient array into individual args matching the lambdify signature.
63: 
64: 3. **Jacobian** — computed via `jax.jacfwd` + `jax.vmap`. Each sample's Jacobian is computed independently and batched.
65: 
66: 4. **Optimization** — `fit_levenberg_marquardt()` in optimize.py solves the damped normal equations. The Jacobian from step 3 feeds directly into the LM step.
67: 
68: ### Data Flow
69: 
70: ```
71: sympy.Expr → JAXModel.__init__() → jax_fun, jac_fun
72:                                 → fit_levenberg_marquardt()
73:                                 → FitResult(coefficients, predictions, cost, ...)
74: ```
75: 
76: ### Key Types
77: 
78: ```python
79: @dataclass
80: class FitResult:
81:     success: bool
82:     coefficients: jnp.ndarray   # optimized coefficients
83:     predictions: jnp.ndarray    # model predictions at optimized coeffs
84:     cost: float                 # sum of squared residuals
85:     n_residuals: int
86:     n_params: int
87:     message: str = ""
88:     nfev: int = 0
89: 
90: @dataclass
91: class EvalResult:
92:     fit: FitResult
93:     score: float        # RMSE
94:     r2: float
95:     evar: float
96:     aic: float
97:     bic: float
98:     chisqr: float
99:     redchi: float
100:     mae: float
101:     rmae: float
102:     predictions: jnp.ndarray
103: ```
104: 
105: ## Gotchas
106: 
107: ### JAX float64
108: 
109: JAX defaults to float32 on most platforms. To use float64 you need:
110: 
111: ```python
112: jax.config.update("jax_enable_x64", True)
113: ```
114: 
115: Or set the env var: `JAX_ENABLE_X64=1`. The current code requests float64 in `jnp.asarray(..., dtype=jnp.float64)` which triggers warnings when x64 is disabled. Tests pass with float32, but precision-sensitive work (e.g., symbolic regression convergence) may need x64.
116: 
117: ### sympy.lambdify + JAX
118: 
119: - `sympy.lambdify` with `modules="jax"` works for most expressions but falls back to numpy on failure.
120: - Each coefficient symbol becomes a separate argument. The wrapper in `JAXModel.jax_fun` unpacks the coefficient array to match.
121: - If the expression has no variables (constant), `jax_fun` receives no input arrays — handle this case.
122: 
123: ### LM Optimizer Convergence
124: 
125: The LM implementation has multiple convergence criteria:
126: 1. Cost below tolerance (`cost < tol`)
127: 2. Relative cost change below tolerance
128: 3. Coefficient change below tolerance
129: 4. Damping blowup (`mu > 1e12`) — failure
130: 
131: The default `tol=1e-4` works for most cases. The float32 precision means you won't get better than ~1e-6 accuracy regardless.
132: 
133: ### Coefficient Symbol Convention
134: 
135: Coefficients are identified by name prefix: `C_` or `C[`. The original pypge used bare `C` with `rewrite_coeff()` to generate `C_0`, `C_1`, etc. The JAX port assumes this convention is already applied. If you create expressions with bare `C` symbols, they won't be extracted as coefficients.
136: 
137: ### Test Precision
138: 
139: Tests use `atol=5e-3` or `rel=5e-3` tolerances because float32 limits precision. Don't tighten these without first ensuring x64 is enabled.
140: 
141: ## Adding New Code
142: 
143: ### New Metric
144: 
145: 1. Add function to `pge_jax/metrics.py` with Google-style docstring
146: 2. Add import and export in `pge_jax/__init__.py`
147: 3. Add to `EvalResult` in `pge_jax/evaluate.py` if it should be part of the full evaluation
148: 4. Add tests in `tests/test_metrics.py`
149: 
150: ### New Optimizer
151: 
152: 1. Add function to `pge_jax/optimize.py` — return `FitResult`
153: 2. Add import in `pge_jax/__init__.py`
154: 3. Wire into `fit_model()` in `pge_jax/evaluate.py` if it should be a first-class option
155: 4. Add tests in `tests/test_optimize.py`
156: 
157: ### New Model Feature
158: 
159: 1. Modify `JAXModel` in `pge_jax/model.py`
160: 2. Update `_build_jax_functions()` if the change affects evaluation
161: 3. Add tests in `tests/test_model.py`
162: 
163: ## PGE Integration (Future)
164: 
165: The `pge_jax` module is the evaluation back-end. The PGE search loop (selection, expansion, prioritization) will be built on top of it. When implementing:
166: 
167: - Use `JAXModel` for all expression evaluation — never call `sympy.lambdify` directly
168: - Use `fit_model()` for the full fit+evaluate pipeline
169: - Use metrics from `pge_jax.metrics` for fitness computation
170: - The `EvalResult` dataclass is the fitness evaluation output — it will feed into NSGA-II selection
171: 
172: ## Reference: pypge
173: 
174: The original implementation lives at https://github.com/verdverm/pypge. Key modules to reference:
175: 
176: - `pypge/model.py` → `pge_jax/model.py` (JAXModel replaces Model)
177: - `pypge/evaluate.py` → `pge_jax/evaluate.py` + `optimize.py` (lmfit → JAX LM)
178: - `pypge/fitness_funcs.py` → `pge_jax/metrics.py` (sklearn metrics → JAX-native)
179: 
180: The PGE search logic (expand.py, search.py, selection.py) is not ported yet — it will be rewritten to use the JAX evaluation pipeline.

(End of file - total 180 lines)
</content>
```

  "newString": "## Reference: pypge (Local)\n\nThe original implementation is at `pypge/pypge/`. Key modules and their port targets:\n\n| pypge module | pge_jax target | Status |\n|---|---|---|\n| `pypge/model.py` (Model class) | Already replaced by `JAXModel` | Done |\n| `pypge/evaluate.py` (Fit/Eval/Score) | `pge_jax/evaluate.py` + `optimize.py` | Done |\n| `pypge/fitness_funcs.py` (multi-obj fitness) | `pge_jax/fitness_funcs.py` | **Not ported** |\n| `pypge/filters.py` (expression filters) | `pge_jax/filters.py` | **Not ported** |\n| `pypge/algebra.py` (expand/factor/simplify) | `pge_jax/algebra.py` | **Not ported** |\n| `pypge/memoize.py` (deduplication) | `pge_jax/memoize.py` | **Not ported** |\n| `pypge/expand.py` (Grower class) | `pge_jax/expand.py` | **Not ported** |\n| `pypge/selection.py` (NSGA-II, SPEA-II) | `pge_jax/selection.py` | **Not ported** |\n| `pypge/search.py` (PGE class, main loop) | `pge_jax/search.py` | **Not ported** |\n| `pypge/parallel.py` (multiprocessing) | `pge_jax/parallel.py` | **Not ported** |\n| `pypge/base.py` / `creator.py` (DEAP fitness) | `pge_jax/base.py` or inline | **Not ported** |\n\n---\n\n## PGE Search Loop — Architecture Reference\n\n### The Full Search Pipeline\n\n```\n                    ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n                    │              PGE.fit(X, Y)                   │\n                    │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────┐  │\n                    │  │           PRELOOP                      │  │\n                    │  │ 1. Generate first_exprs()              │  │\n                    │  │ 2. Filter (remove invalid)             │  │\n                    │  │ 3. Memoize (deduplicate)               │  │\n                    │  │ 4. Algebra (expand/factor)             │  │\n                    │  │ 5. Filter + Memoize again              │  │\n                    │  │ 6. Peek-evaluate OR full-evaluate      │  │\n                    │  │ 7. Push to nsga2_list (population)     │  │\n                    │  │ 8. Push to final (fully evaluated)     │  │\n                    │  └───────────────────────────────────────┘  │\n                    │                                              │\n                    │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────┐  │\n                    │  │           MAIN LOOP (N iterations)     │  │\n                    │  │                                       │  │\n                    │  │  For each expander:                   │  │\n                    │  │    1. heap_pop() — NSGA-II select     │  │\n                    │  │    2. grower.grow() — expand models   │  │\n                    │  │                                       │  │\n                    │  │ 3. Filter expanded models             │  │\n                    │  │ 4. Memoize (deduplicate)              │  │\n                    │  │ 5. Algebra (expand/factor)            │  │\n                    │  │ 6. Filter + Memoize again             │  │\n                    │  │                                       │  │\n                    │  │ 7. Peek-evaluate unique models        │  │\n                    │  │ 8. Push to nsga2_peek heap            │  │\n                    │  │ 9. heap_pop(nsga2_peek)               │  │\n                    │  │ 10. Full-evaluate selected models     │  │\n                    │  │ 11. Push to final                     │  │\n                    │  │ 12. Push to nsga2_list                │  │\n                    │  └───────────────────────────────────────┘  │\n                    │                                              │\n                    │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────┐  │\n                    │  │          FINALIZE                      │  │\n                    │  │ 1. Combine final + nsga2_list         │  │\n                    │  │ 2. sortLogNondominated()              │  │\n                    │  │ 3. Print Pareto fronts                │  │\n                    │  │ 4. Stop workers                       │  │\n                    │  └───────────────────────────────────────┘  │\n                    └─────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### Component Breakdown\n\n#### 1. Expression Model (`pypge/model.py`)\n\nThe `Model` class wraps a sympy expression and manages its lifecycle state. Key attributes:\n\n- **Identification**: `id`, `iter_id`, `parent_id`, `gen_relation` (e.g., \"first_gen\", \"var_xpnd\", \"add_xpnd\", \"mul_xpnd\", \"shrunk\")\n- **Expression**: `orig` (original before coeff rewriting), `expr` (expanded after `rewrite_coeff()`), `pretty` (cached string)\n- **Variables/Coefficients**: `xs` (input variables), `cs` (coefficient symbols `C_0, C_1, ...`), `params` (fitted values)\n- **Size metrics**: `sz` (tree size), `psz` (penalized size, +2 per function node), `jsz`/`jpsz` (Jacobian sizes), `ncs` (num coefficients)\n- **Fitness**: `peek_*` (partial fitness on subset), full `score`, `r2`, `evar`, `aic`, `bic`, `chisqr`, `redchi`, `mae`, `rmae`\n- **Improvement over parent**: `improve_score`, `improve_r2`, etc.\n- **State flags**: `inited`, `memoized`, `algebrad`, `peeked`, `peek_queued`, `peek_popped`, `evaluated`, `popped`, `expanded`, `finalized`, `errored`\n\nKey method: `rewrite_coeff()` — converts bare `sympy.Symbol('C')` leaves into `C_0, C_1, ...` and creates `lmfit.Parameters`. The JAX port's `JAXModel._extract_coeffs_and_vars()` already handles this.\n\n**Size calculation** (`calc_tree_size`): walks `sympy.preorder_traversal`, counts nodes (+2 penalty per `is_Function`), sums integer absolute values as size.\n\n#### 2. Expression Expansion / Grower (`pypge/expand.py`)\n\nThe `Grower` class implements grammar-based expression enumeration. Pre-computed expression pools built in `__init__`:\n\n- **Variable powers**: `xs_pow1` through `xs_pow4` — `x^n`, `x^-n` for n=1..4\n- **Variable products**: `wout_c_xs1_muls` through `wout_c_xs4_muls` — products of 1-4 variables (with replacement)\n- **Coefficient-scaled products**: `with_c_xs1_muls` through `with_c_xs4_muls` — `C * variable_product`\n- **Function expressions**: `wout_c_linear_funcs`, `wout_c_nonlin_funcs`, `with_c_linear_funcs`, `with_c_nonlin_funcs`\n  - Linear: `f(var_product)`, `f(var_product)` with inverse\n  - Nonlinear: `f(C*var_product + C)`, with inverse\n- **Expansion term pools**: `var_sub_terms`, `add_extend_terms`, `mul_extend_terms` — vary by complexity level (low/med/high)\n\n**Key methods:**\n\n- **`first_exprs()`**: Generate initial generation. Combines variable products + function expressions, adds `+C` variants, uniquifies via `evalf()` hashing, wraps in `Model` objects with `gen_relation=\"first_gen\"`\n- **`grow(M)`**: Expand a single model via 5 operators:\n  1. **`_var_sub()`**: Variable substitution — replaces input variable occurrences with more complex expressions (recursive, depth-limited)\n  2. **`_add_extend()`**: Addition extension — adds terms to `Add` nodes (recursive)\n  3. **`_mul_extend()`**: Multiplication extension — adds factors to `Mul` nodes (recursive)\n  4. **`_add_extend_top_level()`**: Top-level addition extension with more complex multiplication (non-recursive)\n  5. **`_shrinker()`**: Term removal from `Add` nodes (recursive)\n- **`_toggle_plus_C(expr)`**: Adds or removes a bare `C` from an addition\n- **`_uniquify(exprs)`**: Removes duplicates via `p.evalf()` hashing\n\n**Policy levels** (all configurable via kwargs):\n- `func_level`: \"linear\" or \"nonlin\" — whether functions use affine transforms `f(C*x+C)` or just `f(x)`\n- `init_level`: \"low\", \"med\", \"high\" — complexity of first-generation models\n- `grow_level` / `subs_level` / `adds_level` / `muls_level`: expansion complexity levels\n- `add_xtop`: Whether to extend at the top level of additions\n- `shrinker`: Whether to try removing terms from additions\n- `limiting_depth`: Depth limit for variable substitution (default 4)\n- `grow_filter`: Whether to avoid duplicate terms in additions\n\n#### 3. Multi-Objective Selection (`pypge/selection.py`)\n\nTaken from DEAP. Key functions:\n\n- **`selNSGA2(individuals, k, nd='standard')`**: NSGA-II selection. Sorts into Pareto fronts, assigns crowding distances, fills selection from best fronts, breaking ties by crowding distance.\n  - `nd='standard'`: Uses `sortNondominated()` (O(M*N^2))\n  - `nd='log'`: Uses `sortLogNondominated()` — **this is what PGE uses**\n- **`sortLogNondominated(individuals, k)`**: Generalized Reduced Run-Time Complexity Non-Dominated Sorting (Fortin et al. 2013). Uses recursive divide-and-conquer with sweep procedures (`sweepA`, `sweepB`) for O(N log^(M-1) N) complexity.\n- **`assignCrowdingDist(individuals)`**: Assigns crowding distance to each individual for diversity maintenance.\n- **`selSPEA2(individuals, k)`**: Strength Pareto EA II selection.\n- **`isDominated(wvalues1, wvalues2)`**: Checks if wvalues1 is dominated by wvalues2 (minimization semantics: lower is better).\n\nFitness objects need `values` attribute (tuple) for `selNSGA2` and `wvalues` attribute for `sortLogNondominated`.\n\n#### 4. Fitness Calculation (`pypge/fitness_funcs.py`)\n\nDynamically constructs multi-objective fitness from parameter list like `[\"normalize\", \"-(1)jpsz\", \"-score\", \"+bic\"]`:\n\n- Weight parsing: `\"-(1)jpsz\"` → weight = -1.0 (minimize jpsz), `\"+bic\"` → weight = +1.0 (maximize bic)\n- `\"normalize\"` prefix: normalizes each objective across the population by L2 norm before setting fitness values\n- `build_value_extractor(params)`: creates a function that extracts specified attributes from each model\n- Fitness values are set via `modl.fitness.setValues(vals)` on DEAP-style fitness objects\n\nFor JAX port, fitness values can be stored directly as tuples on model objects — no DEAP dependency needed.\n\n#### 5. Expression Filters (`pypge/filters.py`)\n\n`default_filters` list applied to every model:\n\n- `filter_too_big`: Removes models with `size() > 64`\n- `filter_has_int_coeff`: Removes expressions with hardcoded integer coefficients (not using `C` symbols)\n- `filter_has_big_pow`: Removes expressions with power exponents > 6\n- `filter_just_C`: Removes expressions that are just the coefficient symbol `C` or a number\n- `filter_no_C`: Removes expressions with no coefficients (constant expressions)\n- `filter_has_coeff_pow`: Removes expressions like `C^2` (coefficient raised to a power)\n\nFilter API: each filter takes `(modl, expr)` and returns `True` if the expression should be **rejected**. Walks `sympy.preorder_traversal(expr)` and checks each node.\n\n#### 6. Algebraic Manipulation (`pypge/algebra.py`)\n\nApplies symbolic simplification to expressions:\n\n- **`manip_model(modl, method)`**: Applies method to model. Returns `(new_model, None)` if expression changed, `(None, \"same\")` if unchanged, `(None, error)` on failure.\n- **`do_simp(expr, method)`**: Supports `\"simplify\"`, `\"expand\"`, `\"factor\"`\n- Methods: `sympy.simplify()`, `sympy.expand()`, `sympy.factor()`\n\n#### 7. Memoization / Deduplication (`pypge/memoize.py`)\n\n- **`Memoizer`**: Indexes models by expression hash. `insert(model)` returns `True` if new, `False` if duplicate. `lookup(model)` returns `(found, model)`.\n- **`Mapper`**: Maps sympy node types to integer codes for serialization (for remote evaluation). Not needed in JAX port — use `hash(expr)` or `expr.__hash__()` directly.\n- In the JAX port, deduplication can use a simple `dict[expr_hash: Expr] -> Model` mapping.\n\n#### 8. The PGE Search Class (`pypge/search.py`)\n\nThe `PGE` class orchestrates everything. Key data structures:\n\n- **`self.models`**: All models ever created (indexed by `id`)\n- **`self.hmap`**: Dict mapping `expr -> Model` for deduplication\n- **`self.final`**: All fully evaluated, finalized models\n- **`self.nsga2_list`**: Models waiting to be expanded (the \"population\" heap)\n- **`self.nsga2_peek`**: Models that have been peek-evaluated, waiting for full evaluation\n- **`self.multi_expanders[i]`**: Per-expander config with `pop_count`, `nsga2_list`, and `grower`\n\n**Main loop per iteration:**\n\n1. **Multi-expand**: For each expander, pop `pop_count` models via NSGA-II selection, call `grower.grow()`, push remaining back\n2. **Filter**: Remove invalid models\n3. **Memoize**: Deduplicate via expression hash\n4. **Algebra**: Apply expand/factor to unique models\n5. **Filter + Memoize** algebraic results again\n6. **Peek-evaluate** unique models on subset of data\n7. **Push** peek'd models to `nsga2_peek` heap\n8. **Pop** best models from peek heap for full evaluation (via NSGA-II selection)\n9. **Full-evaluate** selected models on full training data\n10. **Push** to `self.final` and `nsga2_list`\n\n**Progressive evaluation**: Uses `peek_npts` (default 16) data points for fast partial evaluation, then selects best models from peek heap for full evaluation on all data.\n\n### Data Flow for Each Model\n\n```\n1. Creation: Grower.first_exprs() or Grower.grow() → sympy.Expr\n2. Model wrapping: Model(expr) → rewrite_coeff(), compute Jacobian\n3. Filtering: filters.filter_models() → remove invalid expressions\n4. Deduplication: memoize_models() → check self.hmap[expr]\n5. Algebra: algebra.manip_model() → expand/factor\n6. Deduplication again: after algebra\n7. Peek evaluation: eval_model() on subset of data (fast)\n8. Selection: selNSGA2() or sortLogNondominated() picks best peek'd models\n9. Full evaluation: eval_model() on full data (slow, with lmfit)\n10. Fitness assignment: fitness_funcs.build_fitness_calc() sets model.fitness.values\n11. Population update: push to nsga2_list for future expansion or final for output\n```\n\n### JAX Port Design Decisions\n\nKey differences from pypge for the JAX port:\n\n1. **No DEAP dependency** — fitness values stored directly as tuples on model objects\n2. **No multiprocessing by default** — JAX handles parallelism via XLA; can add later\n3. **No remote evaluation** — all computation is local via JAX\n4. **No lmfit** — replaced by custom JAX-native LM optimizer\n5. **No sklearn** — replaced by JAX-native metrics\n6. **No `lmfit.Parameters`** — coefficients stored as `jnp.ndarray`\n7. **Model class** — can be simplified; state flags are important for the search loop but the DEAP-style fitness wrapper is not needed\n\n### Dependencies\n\nCurrent `pyproject.toml` dependencies:\n- `jax`, `jaxlib` — array computation + autodiff\n- `numpy` — numeric operations\n- `scipy` — for `jax.scipy.optimize.minimize`\n- `sympy` — symbolic expression representation\n- `networkx` — graph storage (for relationship tracking)\n- `tqdm` — progress bars\n\nOptional deps (not needed for core PGE loop):\n- `scikit-learn`, `lmfit`, `pandas` — benchmark/compatibility only\n\n### Porting Order (Recommended)\n\n1. **`filters.py`** — Simple, no dependencies on other new modules\n2. **`algebra.py`** — Simple, only depends on sympy\n3. **`memoize.py`** — Simple hash-based dedup\n4. **`fitness_funcs.py`** — Multi-objective fitness construction (no DEAP needed)\n5. **`selection.py`** — NSGA-II / SPEA-II (standalone, no other new deps)\n6. **`expand.py`** — Grower class (depends on filters for `_uniquify`, creates Model objects)\n7. **`model.py`** — Simplified Model class for the search loop (state tracking, size metrics)\n8. **`search.py`** — PGE class (depends on all above)\n9. **`parallel.py`** — Multiprocessing (optional, can skip initially)"
}
```

```

_Thinking:_

Let me start implementing. I'll write all the modules in dependency order.



**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "\"\"\"Expression validity filters for the PGE search loop.\n\nEach filter takes a ``SearchModel`` and a sympy ``Expr`` and returns\n``True`` if the expression should be **rejected** (removed from the\npopulation).  Filters are applied via\n:func:`filter_models` which walks the full expression tree.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom sympy import preorder_traversal, numbers, Symbol\nfrom sympy.core.numbers import Integer\n\nfrom pge_jax.model import SearchModel\n\nC = Symbol(\"C\")\n\n\ndef filter_models(models: list[SearchModel], filters: list) -> list[SearchModel]:\n    \"\"\"Return only models that pass every filter.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    models:\n        Candidate models to test.\n    filters:\n        List of filter callables.  Each receives ``(model, expr)`` and\n        returns ``True`` to reject.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    list[SearchModel]\n        Models that passed all filters.\n    \"\"\"\n    return [modl for modl in models if not filter_model(modl, modl.orig, filters)]\n\n\ndef filter_model(modl: SearchModel, expr, filters: list) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Walk *expr* tree and return ``True`` if any filter rejects it.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    modl:\n        The model being tested.\n    expr:\n        Sympy expression to check.\n    filters:\n        List of filter callables.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    bool\n        ``True`` if the expression should be rejected.\n    \"\"\"\n    for e in preorder_traversal(expr):\n        for f in filters:\n            if f(modl, e):\n                return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef filter_just_C(modl: SearchModel, expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Reject expressions that are just the bare coefficient symbol ``C`` or a number.\"\"\"\n    if modl.orig is C or modl.orig == C or modl.orig.is_Number:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef filter_no_C(modl: SearchModel, expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Reject expressions with no coefficients (constant expressions).\"\"\"\n    if len(modl.cs) == 0:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef filter_too_big(modl: SearchModel, expr, big: int = 64) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Reject models whose tree size exceeds *big*.\"\"\"\n    if modl.size() > big:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef filter_has_int_coeff(modl: SearchModel, expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Reject expressions with hardcoded integer coefficients (not using ``C`` symbols).\n\n    A coefficient is considered \"hardcoded\" if an ``Add`` or ``Mul`` node\n    has a non-zero / non-one coefficient {
  "content": "\"\"\"Multi-objective selection operators for the PGE search loop.\n\nPorted from DEAP.  Provides NSGA-II, SPEA-II, and tournament selection\nwith dominance + crowding distance. ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef selNSGA2(\n    individuals: List[Any],\n    k: int,\n    nd: str = \"standard\",\n) -> List[Any]:\n    \"\"\"Apply NSGA-II selection operator.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    individuals:\n        List of individuals to select from.\n    k:\n        Number of individuals to select.\n    nd:\n        Non-dominated sorting method: ``\"standard\"`` or ``\"log\"``.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    list\n        Selected individuals (references to input objects).\n    \"\"\"\n    if nd == ValueError(f'selNSGA2: invalid nd method \"{nd}\"')\n\n    for front in pareto_fronts:\n        assignCrowdingDist(front)\n\n    chosen = list(chain(*pareto_fronts[:-1]))\n    k = k - len(chosen)\n chosen.extend(sorted_front[:k])\n\n    return chosen\n\n\ndef sortNondominated(\n    individuals: List[Any],\n    k: int,\n    first_front_only: bool = False,\n) -> List[List[Any]]:\n    \"\"\"Fast non-dominated sorting (Deb et al. 2002).\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    individuals:\n        List of individuals.\n    k:\n        Number of individuals to sort.\n    first_front_only:\n        If ``True``, sort only the first front.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    list[list]\n        List of Pareto fronts (each front is a list of individuals).\n    \"\"\"\n    if k == 0:\n        return []\n\n    map_fit_ind = defaultdict(list)\n    for ind in individuals:\n        map_fit_ind[ind.values].append(ind)\n    fits = list(map_fit_ind.keys())\n\n    current_front = []\n    next_front = []\n    dominating_fits = defaultdict(int)\n    dominated_fits = defaultdict(list)\n\n    for i, fit_i in enumerate(fits):\n        for fit_j in fits[i + 1:]:\n            if fit_i.dominates(fit_j):\n                dominating_fits[fit_j] += 1\n                dominated_fits[fit_i].append(fit_j)\n            elif fit_j.dominates(fit_i):\n                dominating_fits[fit_i] += 1\n                dominated_fits[fit_j].append(fit_i)\n        if dominating_fits[fit_i] == 0:\n            current_front.append(fit_i)\n\n    fronts = [[]]\n    for fit in current_front:\n        fronts[-1].extend(map_fit_ind[fit])\n    pareto_sorted = len(fronts[-1])\n\n    if not first_front_only:\n        N = min(len(individuals), k)\n        while pareto_sorted < N:\n            fronts.append([])\n            for fit_p in current_front:\n                for fit_d in dominated_fits[fit_p]:\n                    dominating_fits[fit_d] -= 1\n                    if fronts[-1].extend(map_fit_ind[fit_d])\n            current_front = next_front\n            next_front = []\n\n    return fronts\n\n\ndef assignCrowdingDist(individuals: List[Any]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Assign crowding distance to each individual.\n\n    Stores the result on ``individual[i].crowding_dist``.\n    \"\"\"\n    if len(individuals) == 0:\n        return\n\n    distances = [0.0] * len(individuals)\n    crowd = [(ind.values, i) for i, ind in enumerate(individuals)]\n\n    nobj = len(individuals[0].values)\n\n    for i in range(nobj):\n        crowd.sort(key=lambda element: element[0][i])\n        distances[crowd[0][1]] = float(\"inf\")\n        distances[crowd[-1][1]] = float(\"inf\")\n        if crowd[-1][0][i] == crowd[0][0][i]:\n            continue\n        norm = nobj * float(crowd[-1][0][i] - crowd[0][0][i])\n        for prev, cur, nxt in zip(crowd[:-2], crowd[1:-1], crowd[2:]):\n            distances[cur[1]] += (nxt[0][i] - prev[0][i]) / norm\n\n    for i, and crowding distance.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    individuals:\n        List of individuals (must have ``crowding_dist`` attribute).\n    k:\n        Number of individuals to select.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    list\n        Selected individuals.\n    \"\"\"\n    def tourn(ind1: Any, ind2: Any) -> Any:\n        if ind1.values.dominates(ind2.values):\n            return ind1\n        if ind2.values.dominates(ind1.values):\n            return ind2\n\n        if getattr(ind1, \"crowding_dist\", 0) < getattr(ind2, \"crowding_dist\", 0):\n            return ind2\n        if getattr(ind1, \"crowding_dist\", 0) > getattr(ind2, \"crowding_dist\", 0):\n            return ind1\n\n        return ind1 if random.random() <= 0.5 else ind2\n\n    individuals_1 = random.sample(individuals, len(individuals))\n    individuals_2 = random.sample(individuals, len(individuals))\n\n    chosen = []\n    for i in range(0, k, 4):\n        chosen.append(tourn(individuals_1[i], individuals_1[i + 1]))\n        chosen.append(tourn(individuals_1[i + 2], individuals_1[i + 3]))\n        chosen.append(tourn(individuals_2[i], individuals_2[i + 1]))\n        chosen.append(tourn(individuals_2[i + 2], individuals_2[i + 3]))\n\n    return chosen\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Generalized Reduced Run-Time Complexity Non-Dominated Sorting\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef identity(obj: Any) -> Any:\n    \"\"\"Return *obj* directly.\"\"\"\n    return obj\n\n\ndef isDominated(wvalues1: Tuple[float, ...], wvalues2: Tuple[float, ...]) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if *wvalues1* is dominated by *wvalues2*.\n\n    Minimization semantics: lower is better.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    wvalues1:\n        Fitness values that would be dominated.\n    wvalues2:\n        Dominant fitness values.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    bool\n        ``True`` if wvalues2 dominates wvalues1.\n    \"\"\"\n    not_equal = False\n    for self_w, other_w in zip(wvalues1, wvalues2):\n        if self_w > other_w:\n            return False\n        if self_w < other_w:\n            not_equal = True\n    return not_equal\n\n\ndef median(seq: Sequence[Any], key=identity) -> Any:\n    \"\"\"Return the median value of *seq*.\"\"\"\n    sseq = sorted(seq, key=key)\n    length = len(seq)\n    if length % 2 == 1:\n        return key(sseq[(length - 1) // 2])\n    return (key(sseq[(length - 1) // 2]) + key(sseq[length // 2])) / 2.0\n\n\ndef sortLogNondominated(\n    individuals: List[Any],\n    k: int,\n    first_front_only: bool = False,\n) -> List[List[Any]]:\n    \"\"\"Generalized Reduced Run-Time Complexity Non-Dominated Sorting.\n\n    Uses the algorithm of Fortin et al. (2013).\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    individuals:\n        List of individuals (must have ``wvalues`` attribute).\n    k:\n        Number of individuals to sort.\n    first_front_only:\n        If ``True``, return only the first front.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    list[list]\n        List of Pareto fronts.\n    \"\"\"\n    if k == 0:\n        return []\n\n    unique_fits = defaultdict(list)\n    for i, ind in enumerate(individuals):\n        unique_fits[ind.wvalues].append(ind)\n\n    obj = len(individuals[0].wvalues) - 1\n    fitnesses = list(unique_fits.keys())\n    front = dict.fromkeys(fitnesses, 0)\n\n    fitnesses.sort(reverse=True)\n    sortNDHelperA(fitnesses, obj, front)\n\n    nbfronts = max(front.values()) + 1\n    pareto_fronts = [[] for _ in range(nbfronts)]\n    for fit in fitnesses:\n        index = front[fit]\n        pareto_fronts[index].extend(unique_fits[fit])\n\n    if not first_front_only:\n        count = 0\n        for i, front in enumerate(pareto_fronts):\n            count += len(front)\n            if count >= k:\n                return pareto_fronts[: i + 1]\n        return pareto_fronts\n    return pareto_fronts[0]\n\n\ndef sortNDHelperA(fitnesses: List, obj: int, front: dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Non-dominated sort on the first M objectives.\"\"\"\n    if len(fitnesses) < 2:\n        return\n    if len(fitnesses) == 2:\n        s1, s2 = fitnesses[0], fitnesses[1]\n        if isDominated(s2[: obj + 1], s1[: obj + 1]):\n            front[s2] = max(front[s2], front[s1] + 1)\n    elif obj == 1:\n        sweepA(fitnesses, front)\n    elif len(frozenset(map(itemgetter(obj), fitnesses))) == 1:\n        sortNDHelperA(fitnesses, obj - 1, front)\n    else:\n        best, worst = splitA(fitnesses, obj)\n        sortNDHelperA(best, obj, front)\n        sortNDHelperB(best, worst, obj - 1, front)\n        sortNDHelperA(worst, obj, front)\n\n\ndef splitA(fitnesses: List, obj: int) -> Tuple[List, List]:\n    \"\"\"Partition fitnesses according to the median of objective *obj*.\"\"\"\n    median_ = median(fitnesses, itemgetter(obj))\n    best_a, worst_a, best_b, worst_b = [], [], [], []\n\n    for fit in fitnesses:\n        if fit[obj] > median_:\n            best_a.append(fit)\n            best_b.append(fit)\n        elif fit[obj] < median_:\n            worst_a.append(fit)\n            worst_b.append(fit)\n        else:\n            best_a.append(fit)\n            worst_b.append(fit)\n\n    balance_a = abs(len(best_a) - len(worst_a))\n    balance_b = abs(len(best_b) - len(worst_b))\n\n    if balance_a <= balance_b:\n        return best_a, worst_a\n    return best_b, worst_b\n\n\ndef sweepA(fitnesses: List, front: dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Update front numbers using a geometric sweep on the first 2 objectives.\"\"\"\n    stairs = [-fitnesses[0][1]]\n    fstairs = [fitnesses[0]]\n    for fit in fitnesses[1:]:\n        idx = bisect.bisect_right(stairs, -fit[1])\n        if 0 < idx <= len(stairs):\n            fstair = max(fstairs[:idx], key=front.__getitem__)\n            front[fit] = max(front[fit], front[fstair] + 1)\n        for i, fstair in enumerate(fstairs[idx:], idx):\n            if front[fstair] == front[fit]:\n                del stairs[i]\n                del fstairs[i]\n                break\n        stairs.insert(idx, -fit[1])\n        fstairs.insert(idx, fit)\n\n\ndef sortNDHelperB(best: List, worst: List, obj: int, front: dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Assign front numbers to solutions in *worst* based on *best*.\"\"\"\n    key = itemgetter(obj)\n    if len(worst) == 0 or len(best) == 0:\n        return\n    if len(best) == 1 or len(worst) == 1:\n        for hi in worst:\n            for li in best:\n                if isDominated(hi[: obj + 1], li[: obj + 1]) or hi[: obj + 1] == li[: obj + 1]:\n                    front[hi] = max(front[hi], front[li] + 1)\n    elif obj == 1:\n        sweepB(best, worst, front)\n    elif key(min(best, key=key)) >= key(max(worst, key=key)):\n        sortNDHelperB(best, worst, obj - 1, front)\n    elif key(max(best, key=key)) >= key(min(worst, key=key)):\n        best1, best2, front)\n\n\ndef splitB(\n    best: List, worst: List, obj: int\n) -> Tuple[List, List, List, List]:\n    \"\"\"Split both best and worst sets according to the median.\"\"\"\n    median_ = median(best if len(best) > len(worst) else worst, itemgetter(obj))\n    best1_a, best2_a, best1_b, best2_b = [], [], [], []\n    for fit in best:\n        if fit[obj] > median_:\n            best1_a.append(fit)\n            best1_b.append(fit)\n        elif fit[obj] < median_:\n            best2_a.append(fit)\n            best2_b.append(fit)\n        else:\n            best1_a.append(fit)\n            best2_b.append(fit)\n\n    worst1_a, worst2_a, worst1_b, worst2_b = [], [], [], []\n    for fit in worst:\n        if fit[obj] > median_:\n            worst1_a.append(fit)\n            worst1_b.append(fit)\n        elif fit[obj] < median_:\n            worst2_a.append(fit)\n            worst2_b.append(fit)\n        else:\n            worst1_a.append(fit)\n            worst2_b.append(fit)\n\n    balance_a = abs(len(best1_a) - len(best2_a) + len(worst1_a) - len(worst2_a))\n    balance_b = abs(len(best1_b) - len(best2_b) + len(worst1_b) - len(worst2_b))\n\n    if balance_a <= balance_b:\n        return best1_a, best2_a, worst1_a, worst2_a\n    return best1_b, best2_b, worst1_b, worst2_b\n\n\ndef sweepB(best: List, worst: List, front: dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Adjust rank of worst fitnesses based on best on first 2 objectives.\"\"\"\n    stairs, fstairs = [], []\n    iter_best = iter(best)\n    next_best = next(iter_best, False)\n    for h in worst:\n        while next_best and h[:2] <= next_best[:2]:\n            insert = True\n            for i, fstair in enumerate(fstairs):\n                if front[fstair] == front[next_best]:\n                    if fstair[1] > next_best[1]:\n                        insert = False\n                    else:\n                        del stairs[i], fstairs[i]\n                    break\n            if insert:\n                idx = bisect.bisect_right(stairs, -next_best[1])\n                stairs.insert(idx, -next_best[1])\n                fstairs.insert(idx, next_best)\n            next_best = max(front[h], front[fstair] + 1)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# SPEA-II\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef selSPEA2(individuals: List[Any], k: int) -> List[Any]:\n    \"\"\"Apply SPEA-II selection operator.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    individuals:\n        List of individuals.\n    k:\n        Number of individuals to select.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    list\n        Selected individuals.\n    \"\"\"\n    N = len(individuals)\n    L = len(individuals[0].values)\n    K = math.sqrt(N)\n    strength_fits = [0] * N\n    fits = [0] * N\n    dominating_inds = [list() for _ in range(N)]\n\n    for i, ind_i in enumerate(individuals):\n        for j, ind_j in enumerate(individuals[i + 1:], i + 1):\n            if ind_i.values.dominates(ind_j.values):\n                strength_fits[i] += 1\n                dominating_inds[j].append(i)\n            elif ind_j.values.dominates(ind_i.values):\n                strength_fits[j] += 1\n                dominating_inds[i].append(j)\n\n    for i in                 for l in range(L)\n                )\n                distances[j] = dist\n            kth_dist = _randomizedSelect(distances, 0, N - 1, K)\n            density = 1.0 / (kth_dist + next_indices[: k - len(chosen_indices)]]\n\n    elif len(chosen_indices) > k:\n        N_chosen = len(chosen_indices)\n        distances = [[0.0] * N_chosen for _ in range(N_chosen)]\n in range(1, N_chosen):\n                l = j\n                while (\n                    l > 0\n                    and distances[i][j]\n                    < distances[i][sorted_indices[i][l - 1]]\n                ):\n                    sorted_indices[i][l] = sorted_indices[i][l - 1]\n                    l -= 1\n                sorted_indices[i][l] = j\n\n        size = N_chosen\n 11: def _extract_coeffs_and_vars(
12:     expr: sympy.Expr,
13: ) -> tuple[list[sympy.Symbol], list[sympy.Symbol]]:
14:     """Pull coefficient (C_*) and variable symbols from *expr*.
15: 
16:     Convention: symbols whose name starts with ``C`` (but is not
17:     exactly ``'C'``) are treated as coefficients.  Everything else
18:     that appears free in the expression is an input variable.
19: 
20:     Both lists are sorted by string name for deterministic ordering.
21:     """
22:     coeffs: list[sympy.Symbol] = []
23:     vars_: list[sympy.Symbol] = []
24:     for sym in expr.free_symbols:
25:         name = str(sym)
26:         if name.startswith("C_") or name.startswith("C["):
27:             coeffs.append(sym)
28:         else:
29:             vars_.append(sym)
30:     coeffs.sort(key=lambda s: str(s))
31:     vars_.sort(key=lambda s: str(s))
32:     return coeffs, vars_
