35: class JAXModel:
36:     """Wraps a sympy expression and provides JAX-compatible evaluation.
37: 
38:     This is the JAX equivalent of pypge's ``Model`` class, but replaces
39:     the ``sympy.lambdify`` + ``lmfit`` evaluation pipeline with
40:     JAX-native code.
41: 
42:     Parameters
43:     ----------
44:     expr:
45:         A sympy expression.  Bare ``sympy.Symbol('C')`` leaves are
46:         treated as optimisable coefficients; all other free symbols
47:         are treated as input variables.
48:     cs:
49:         Explicit list of coefficient symbols.  If *None* they are
50:         inferred from *expr*.
51:     xs:
52:         Explicit list of input-variable symbols.  If *None* they are
53:         inferred from *expr*.
54:     c_values:
55:         Initial coefficient values (used only to build the JAX
56:         function; the optimiser will overwrite them).
57: 
58:     Attributes
59:     ----------
60:     orig : sympy.Expr
61:         The original expression before expansion.
62:     expr : sympy.Expr
63:         ``sympy.expand(orig)``.
64:     cs : list[sympy.Symbol]
65:         Coefficient symbols, ordered consistently.
66:     xs : list[sympy.Symbol]
67:         Input-variable symbols, ordered consistently.
68:     n_coeffs : int
69:         Number of optimisable coefficients.
70:     n_vars : int
71:         Number of input variables.
72:     jax_fun : callable
73:         JAX-traceable function ``(cs, *xs) -> prediction``.
74:     jac_fun : callable
75:         JAX-traceable function ``(cs, *xs) -> Jacobian matrix``
76:         of shape ``(n_samples, n_coeffs)``.
77:     """
78: 
79:     def __init__(
80:         self,
81:         expr: sympy.Expr,
82:         cs: Sequence[sympy.Symbol] | None = None,
83:         xs: Sequence[sympy.Symbol] | None = None,
84:         c_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
85:     ):
86:         self.orig = expr
87:         self.expr = sympy.expand(expr)
88: 
89:         if cs is None:
90:             cs, xs = _extract_coeffs_and_vars(self.expr)
91:         self.cs = list(cs)
92:         self.xs = list(xs) if xs is not None else []
93:         self.n_coeffs = len(self.cs)
94:         self.n_vars = len(self.xs)
95: 
96:         if c_values is not None:
97:             c_vals = np.asarray(c_values, dtype=np.float64)
98:             if self.n_coeffs > 0 and len(c_vals) != self.n_coeffs:
99:                 raise ValueError(f"c_values length ({len(c_vals)}) != n_coeffs ({self.n_coeffs})")
100:             self.c_values = c_vals
101:         else:
102:             self.c_values = np.zeros(self.n_coeffs, dtype=np.float64)
103: 
104:         self._build_jax_functions()
105: 
106:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
107:     # JAX function construction
108:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
109: 
110:     def _build_jax_functions(self) -> None:
111:         """Lambdify the expression with the ``jax`` module and wrap it."""
112:         all_syms = self.cs + self.xs
113: 
114:         if len(all_syms) == 0:
115:             # Truly constant expression
116:             val = float(self.expr)
117:             const_val = jnp.array(val)
118: 
119:             def jax_fun(coefs: jnp.ndarray, *inputs: jnp.ndarray) -> jnp.ndarray:
120:                 shape = inputs[0].shape if inputs else ()
121:                 return jnp.broadcast_to(const_val, shape)
122: 
123:             def jac_fun(coefs: jnp.ndarray, *inputs: jnp.ndarray) -> jnp.ndarray:
124:                 shape = inputs[0].shape if inputs else (1,)
125:                 return jnp.zeros((len(shape) if isinstance(shape, tuple) else 1, 0))
126: 
127:             self.jax_fun = jax_fun
128:             self.jac_fun = jac_fun
129:             return
130: 
131:         # Lambdify with JAX backend
132:         try:
133:             raw_fun = sympy.lambdify(all_syms, self.expr, modules="jax")
134:         except Exception:
135:             raw_fun = sympy.lambdify(all_syms, self.expr, modules="numpy")
136: 
137:         # Wrap so the first arg is the coefficient array, the rest are
138:         # input-variable arrays.  This matches the signature expected
139:         # by the optimiser and Jacobian builder.
140:         def jax_fun(coefs: jnp.ndarray, *inputs: jnp.ndarray) -> jnp.ndarray:
141:             args: list[jnp.ndarray] = []
142:             if self.n_coeffs > 0:
143:                 # Each coefficient symbol needs its own argument
144:                 for i in range(self.n_coeffs):
145:                     args.append(coefs[i])
146:             args.extend(inputs)
147:             result = raw_fun(*args)
148:             result = jnp.asarray(result, dtype=jnp.float64)
149:             # Ensure output shape matches input data shape
150:             if result.ndim == 0:
151:                 if inputs:
152:                     result = jnp.broadcast_to(result, inputs[0].shape)
153:                 # else keep as scalar
154:             return result
155: 
156:         # Jacobian via jax.jacfwd + vmap
157:         if self.n_coeffs > 0:
158: 
159:             def _pred_single(coefs: jnp.ndarray, x0: jnp.ndarray) -> jnp.ndarray:
160:                 if self.n_vars == 0:
161:                     return jnp.zeros_like(x0)
162:                 return jax_fun(coefs, x0)
163: 
164:             jac_raw = jax.jacfwd(_pred_single, argnums=0)
165: 
166:             def jac_fun(coefs: jnp.ndarray, *inputs: jnp.ndarray) -> jnp.ndarray:
167:                 if self.n_vars == 0:
168:                     n = inputs[0].shape[0] if inputs else 1
169:                     return jnp.zeros((n, self.n_coeffs))
170:                 # vmap over data points
171:                 jac_sampled = jax.vmap(jac_raw, in_axes=(None, 0))
172:                 return jac_sampled(coefs, inputs[0])
173: 
174:             self.jac_fun = jac_fun
175:         else:
176: 
177:             def jac_fun(coefs: jnp.ndarray, *inputs: jnp.ndarray) -> jnp.ndarray:
178:                 if inputs:
179:                     n = inputs[0].shape[0]
180:                 else:
181:                     n = 1
182:                 return jnp.zeros((n, 0))
183: 
184:         self.jax_fun = jax_fun
185:         self.jac_fun = jac_fun
186: 
187:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
188:     # Convenience methods
189:     # ------------------------------------------------------------------
190: 
191:     def predict(self, coefs: jnp.ndarray, *inputs: jnp.ndarray) -> jnp.ndarray:
192:         """Evaluate the expression at *inputs* with given coefficients."""
193:         return self.jax_fun(coefs, *inputs)
194: 
195:     def jacobian(self, coefs: jnp.ndarray, *inputs: jnp.ndarray) -> jnp.ndarray:
196:         """Jacobian of predictions w.r.t. coefficients.
197: 
198:         Returns an array of shape ``(n_samples, n_coeffs)``.
199:         """
200:         return self.jac_fun(coefs, *inputs)

204:         subs = dict(zip(self.cs, coefs.tolist() if self.n_coeffs > 0 else []))

Integer leaf values are added\n        as their absolute value.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        tuple[int, int]\n            ``(size, penalised_size)``.\n        \"\"\"\n        i = 0\n        p = 0\n        for e in sympy.preorder_traversal(self.expr):\n            if e.is_Integer:\n                i += int(abs(e))\n                continue\n            if e.is_Function:\n                p += 2\n            i += 1\n        return i, i + p\n\n    def calc_jac_size(self) -> Tuple[int, int]:\n        \"\"\"Compute Jacobian size and penalised Jacobian size.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        tuple[int, int]\n            ``(size, penalised_size)``.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Build the Jacobian symbolically\n        if len(self.cs) == 0:\n            return 0, 0\n        jac_exprs = [sympy.diff(self.expr, c) for c in self.cs]\n        i, p = 0, 0\n        for jac in jac_exprs:\n            for e in sympy.preorder_traversal(jac):\n                if e.is_Integer:\n                    i += int(abs(e))\n                    continue\n                if e.is_Function:\n                    p += 2\n                i += 1\n        return i, i + p\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Coefficient rewriting (converts bare C to C_0, C_1, ...)\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def rewrite_coeff(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Rewrite bare ``sympy.Symbol('C')`` into ``C_0, C_1, ...``.\n\n        Replaces all bare ``C`` atoms in ``self.orig`` with\n        sequentially-numbered coefficient symbols, updates\n        ``self.expr`` and ``self.cs``, and builds the JAX wrapper.\n        \"\"\"\n        C = sympy.Symbol(\"C\")\n        ii = 0\n        expr, ii = self._rewrite_coeff_helper(self.orig, 0)\n        self.expr = expr\n        self.cs = [sympy.Symbol(f\"C_{i}\") for i in range(ii)]\n        self.ncs = len(self.cs)\n\n        # Build JAX wrapper\n        self.jax_model = JAXModel(expr, cs=self.cs, xs=self.xs)\n\n    def _rewrite_coeff_helper(self, expr, ii: int):\n        \"\"\"Recursive helper for :meth:`rewrite_coeff`.\"\"\"\n        ret = expr\n        if not expr.is_Atom:\n            args = []\n            for e in expr.args:\n                if not e.is_Atom:\n                    ee, ii = self._rewrite_coeff_helper(e, ii)\n                    args.append(ee)\n                elif e == sympy.Symbol(\"C\"):\n                    args.append(sympy.Symbol(f\"C_{ii}\"))\n                    ii += 1\n                else:\n                    args.append(e)\n            args = tuple(args)\n            ret = expr.func(*args)\n        return ret, ii\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Fitness comparison helpers\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def dominates(self, other: \"SearchModel\") -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if this model dominates *other* in fitness.\n\n        Uses weighted fitness values (``wvalues``).  A model dominates\n        another if it is no worse in all objectives and strictly better\n        in at least one (minimisation semantics: lower is better).\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        other:\n            Another model to compare against.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        bool\n            ``True`` if this model dominates *other*.\n        \"\"\"\n        if not hasattr(other, \"wvalues\") or not self.wvalues:\n            return False\n        not_equal = False\n        for self_w, other_w in zip(self.wvalues, other.wvalues):\n            if self_w > other_w:\n                return False\n            if self_w < other_w:\n                not_equal = True\n        return not_equal\n",

  "content": "\"\"\"Expression expansion (Grower) for the PGE search loop.\n\nImplements grammar-based expression enumeration. Supported keys:\n\n        func_level : str\n            ``\"linear\"`` or ``\"nonlin\"`` — affine transforms or not.\n        init_level : str\n            ``\"low\"``, ``\"med\"``, ``\"high\"`` — first-gen complexity.\n        grow_level : str\n            ``\"low\"``, ``\"med\"``, ``\"high\"`` — expansion complexity.\n        subs_level : str\n            Variable substitution complexity.\n        adds_level : str\n            Addition extension complexity.\n        muls_level : str\n            Multiplication extension complexity.\n        add_xtop : bool\n            Extend at top level of additions.\n        shrinker : bool\n            Try removing terms from additions.\n        limiting_depth : int\n            Depth limit for variable substitution (default 4).\n        grow_filter : bool\n            Avoid duplicate terms in additions.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        xs,\n        funcs: Optional[List],\n        **kwargs,\n    ):\n        # Normalise single symbol to list\n        if isinstance(xs, sympy.Symbol):\n            xs = [xs]\n        self.xs = xs\n        self.funcs = funcs\n\n        # Policy defaults\n self.grow_filter: bool = False\n        self.grow_level: str = \"low\"\n        self.subs_level: str = \"low\"\n        self.adds_level: str = \"low\"\n        self.muls_level: str = \"low\"\n\n        # Apply kwargs overrides\n        for key, value in kwargs.items():\n            setattr(self, key, value)\n\n        # Build pre-computed expression pools\n        self._build_pools()\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Pool construction\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _build_pools(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Build all pre-computed expression pools.\"\"\"\n        # Variable powers: x^n, x^-n for n=1..4\n        self.xs_pow1: list = [\n            x ** (n * (p + 1))\n            for p in range(1)\n            for n in [-1, 1]\n            for x in self.xs\n        ]\n        self.xs_pow2: list = [\n            x ** (n * (p + 1))\n            for p in range(2)\n            for n in [-1, 1]\n            for x in self.xs\n        ]\n        self.xs_pow3: list = [\n            x ** (n * (p + 1))\n            for p in range(3)\n            for n in [-1, 1]\n            for x in self.xs\n        ]\n        self.xs_pow4: list = [\n            x ** (n * (p + 1))\n            for p in range(4)\n            for n in [-1, 1]\n            for x in self.xs\n        ]\n\n        # Variable products (without coefficient)\n        self.wout_c_xs1_muls: list = list(self.xs_pow1)\n        self.wout_c_xs2_muls: list = (\n            [a * b for a, b in combos_withR(self.xs_pow1, 2)] + self.wout_c_xs1_muls\n        )\n        self.wout_c_xs3_muls: list = (\n            [a * b * c for a, b, c in combos_withR(self.xs_pow1, 3)]\n            + self.wout_c_xs2_muls\n        )\n        self.wout_c_xs4_muls: list = (\n            [a * b * c * d for a, b, c, d in combos_withR(self.xs_pow1, 4)]\n            + self.wout_c_xs3_muls\n        )\n        self.wout_c_xs3_muls = self._uniquify(self.wout_c_xs3_muls)\n\n        # Coefficient-scaled variable products\n        self.with_c_xs1_muls: list = [C * m for m in self.wout_c_xs1_muls]\n        self.with_c_xs2_muls: list = [C * m for m in self.wout_c_xs2_muls]\n        self.with_c_xs3_muls: list = [C * m for m in self.wout_c_xs3_muls]\n        self.with_c_xs4_muls: list = [C * m for m in self.wout_c_xs4_muls]\n\n        # Function expressions\n        if self.funcs is not None:\n            self.wout_c_linear_funcs: list = [\n                f(x) for f in self.funcs for x in self.wout_c_xs1_muls\n            ]\n            self.wout_c_nonlin_funcs: list = [\n                f(C * x + C) for f in self.funcs for x in self.wout_c_xs1_muls\n            ]\n            self.with_c_linear_funcs: list = [\n                f(x) for f in self.funcs for x in self.wout_c_xs1_muls\n            ]\n            self.with_c_nonlin_funcs: list = [\n                f(C * x + C) for f in self.funcs for x in self.wout_c_xs1_muls\n            ]\n        else:\n            self.wout_c_linear_funcs = []\n            self.wout_c_nonlin_funcs = []\n            self.with_c_linear_funcs = []\n            self.with_c_nonlin_funcs =   base = self.with_c_linear_funcs\n            alt = self.wout_c_linear_funcs\n        elif self.func_level in (\"nonlin\", \"nonlinear\"):\n            base = self.with_c_nonlin_funcs\n            alt = self.wout_c_nonlin_funcs\n        else:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unknown func_level: {self.func_level!r}\")\n\n        self.with_c_func_exprs = base + [f ** (-1) for f in base]\n        self.wout_c_func_exprs = alt + [f ** (-1) for f in alt]\n\n        # Expansion term pools\n        self.init_var_subs()\n        self.init_add_extends()\n        self.init_mul_extends()\n\n    def list(self.wout_c_xs2_muls)\n        self.var_sub_dep_terms = (\n            self.var_sub_dep_lim_terms + list(self.wout_c_func_exprs)\n        )\n\n        if self.subs_level == \"low\":\n            self.var_sub_lim_terms = list(self.wout_c_xs2_muls)\n            self.var_sub_terms = (\n                self.var_sub_lim_terms + list(self.wout_c_func_exprs)\n            )\n        elif self.subs_level == \"med\":\n            self.var_sub_lim_terms = list(self.wout_c_xs2_muls) + add_terms\n            self.var_sub_terms = (\n                self.var_sub_lim_terms + list(self.wout_c_func_exprs)\n            )\n        elif self.subs_level == \"high\":\n            self.var_sub_dep_lim_terms += add_terms\n            self.var_sub_dep_terms += add_terms\n list(self.wout_c_func_exprs)\n            )\n        else:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unknown subs_level: {self.subs_level!r}\")\n\n        self.var_sub_terms = self._uniquify(self.var_sub_terms)\n        self.var_sub_lim_terms = self._uniquify(self.var_sub_lim_terms)\n\n    def init_add_extends(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Build addition extension term pools.\"\"\"\n        if self.adds_level == \"low\":\n            self.add_extend_lim_terms = list(self.with_c_xs1_muls)\n            self.add_extend_terms = (\n                list(self.with_c_xs1_muls) + list(self.with_c_func_exprs)\n            )\n        elif self.adds_level == \"med\":\n            self.add_extend_lim_terms = list(self.with_c_xs2_muls)\n            self.add_extend_terms = (\n                list(self.with_c_xs2_muls) + list(self.with_c_func_exprs)\n            )\n        elif self.adds_level == \"high\":\n            self.add_extend_lim_terms = list(self.with_c_xs2_muls)\n                + list(self.with_c_func_exprs)\n                + cross\n            )\n        else:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unknown adds_level: init_mul_extends(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Build multiplication extension term pools.\"\"\"\n        if self.muls_level == \"low\":\n            self.mul_extend_lim_terms = list(self.wout_c_xs1_muls)\n            self.mul_extend_terms = (\n                list(self.wout_c_xs1_muls) + list(self.wout_c_func_exprs)\n            )\n        elif self.muls_level == \"med\":\n            self.mul_extend_lim_terms = list(self.wout_c_xs2_muls)\n            self.mul_extend_terms = (\n                list(self.wout_c_xs2_muls) + list(self.wout_c_func_exprs)\n            )\n        elif self.muls_level == \"high\":\n            self.mul_extend_lim_terms = list(self.wout_c_xs2_muls)\n            cross = [x * f for f in self.wout_c_func_exprs for x in self.wout_c_xs1_muls]\n            self.mul_extend_terms = (\n                list(self.wout_c_xs2_muls)\n                + list(self.wout_c_func_exprs)\n                + cross\n            )\n        else:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unknown muls_level: {self.muls_level!r}\")\n\n        self.mul_extend_terms = self._uniquify(self.mul_extend_terms)\n        self.mul_extend_lim_terms = self._uniquify(self.mul_extend_lim_terms)\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Public API\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def first_exprs(self) -> List[SearchModel]:\n        \"\"\"Generate the initial generation of models.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        list[SearchModel]\n            First-generation models with ``gen_relation=\"first_gen\"``.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.init_level == \"low\":\n            if len(self.xs) > 3:\n                mul_exprs = self.with_c_xs1_muls\n            else:\n                mul_exprs = self.with_c_xs2_muls\n        elif self.init_level == \"med\":\n            if len(self.xs) > 3:\n                mul_exprs = self.with_c_xs1_muls + self.with_c_func_exprs\n            elif len(self.xs) > 1:\n                mul_exprs = self.with_c_xs2_muls + self.with_c_func_exprs\n            else:\n                mul_exprs = self.with_c_xs3_muls + self.with_c_func_exprs\n        elif self.init_level == \"high\":\n            if len(self.xs) > 3:\n                mul_exprs = self.with_c_xs2_muls + self.with_c_func_exprs\n            elif len(self.xs) > 1:\n                mul_exprs = self.with_c_xs3_muls + self.with_c_func_exprs\n            else:\n                mul_exprs = self.with_c_xs4_muls + self.with_c_func_exprs\n        else:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unknown init_level: {self.init_level!r}\")\n\n        mid_exprs = mul_exprs\n        add_exprs = [a + b for a, b in combos_woutR(mid_exprs, 2)]\n        if self.init_level == \"high\":\n            add_exprs += [\n                a + b + c for a, b, c in combos_woutR(mid_exprs, 3)\n            ]\n\n        exprs_set = mid_exprs + add_exprs + self.with_c_func_exprs\n\n        # Always add the +C variants\n        plus_C_exprs = [sympy.Add(expr, C) for expr in exprs_set]\n        ret_exprs = exprs_set + plus_C_exprs\n\n        # Uniquify\n        ret_exprs = self._uniquify(ret_exprs)\n\n        models = [SearchModel(e, xs=self.xs) for e in ret_exprs]\n        for m in models:\n            m.gen_relation = \"first_gen\"\n            m.parent_id = -1\n            m.rewrite_coeff()  # Build JAX wrapper\n\n        return models\n\n    def grow(self, M: SearchModel) -> List[SearchModel]:\n        \"\"\"Expand a single model via all growth operators.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        M:\n            Model to expand.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        list[SearchModel]\n            Child models from all expansion operators.\n        \"\"\"\n        var_expands = self._var_sub(M.orig)\n        add_expands = self._add_extend(M.orig)\n        mul_expands = self._mul_extend(M.orig)\n\n        var_expands_C = [self._toggle_plus_C(e) for e in var_expands]\n        add_expands_C = [self._toggle_plus_C(e) for e in add_expands]\n        mul_expands_C = [self._toggle_plus_C(e) for e in mul_expands]\n\n        var_expands = self._uniquify(var_expands + var_expands_C)\n        add_expands = self._uniquify(add_expands + add_expands_C)\n        mul_expands = self._uniquify(mul_expands + mul_expands_C)\n\n        add_biggers = []\n        if self.add_xtop:\n            add_biggers = self._add_extend_top_level(M.orig)\n            add_biggers_C = [self._toggle_plus_C(e) for e in add_biggers]\n            add_biggers = self._uniquify(add_biggers + add_biggers_C)\n\n        shrunk = []\n        if self.shrinker:\n            shrunk = self._shrinker(M.orig)\n\n        var_models = [\n            SearchModel(e, p_id=M.id, reln=\"var_xpnd\")\n            for e in var_expands\n            if e != C\n        ]\n in mul_expands\n            if e != C\n        ]\n        shrunk_models = [\n            SearchModel(e, p_id=M.id, reln=\"shrunk\")\n            for e in shrunk\n            if e != C\n        ]\n\n        return var_models + big_models + add_models + mul_models + shrunk_models\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Expansion operators\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _var_sub(\n        self, expr, limit_sub: bool = False, depth: int = 1\n    ) -> list:\n        \"\"\"Variable substitution — replace input variables with complex terms.\"\"\"\n        new_exprs: list = []\n\n        if expr.is_Atom:\n            return new_exprs\n\n        args_sets: list = []\n        for i, e in enumerate(expr.args):\n            if not e.is_Atom:\n                lim_sub = limit_sub or not (e.is_Add or e.is_Mul)\n                ee = self._var_sub(e, lim_sub, depth=depth + 1)\n                if len(ee) > 0:\n                    args_map = set(expr.args)\n                    for vs in ee:\n                        if self.grow_filter and expr.is_Add and vs in args_map:\n                            continue\n                        cloned_args = list(expr.args)\n                        cloned_args[i] = vs\n                        args_sets.append(cloned_args)\n            elif e in self.xs:\n                sub_terms = None\n                if depth >= self.limiting_depth:\n                    sub_terms = self.var_sub_dep_terms\n                else:\n                    sub_terms = self.var_sub_terms\n                if limit_sub:\n                    if depth >= self.limiting_depth:\n                        sub_terms = self.var_sub_dep_lim_terms\n                    else:\n                        sub_terms = self.var_sub_lim_terms\n\n                for vs in sub_terms:\n                    cloned_args = list(expr.args)\n                    cloned_args[i] = vs\n                    args_sets.append(cloned_args)\n\n        for args in args_sets:\n            args = tuple(args)\n            tmp = expr.func(*args)\n            new_exprs.append(tmp)\n\n        return self._uniquify(new_exprs)\n\n    def _add_extend(\n        self, expr, limit_sub: bool = False\n    ) -> list:\n        \"\"\"Addition extension — add terms to Add nodes.\"\"\"\n        new_exprs: list = []\n\n        if expr.is_Atom:\n            return new_exprs\n\n        args_sets: list = []\n\n        if expr.is_Add:\n            sub_terms = self.add_extend_terms\n            if limit_sub:\n                sub_terms = self.add_extend_lim_terms\n            args_map = set(expr.args)\n            for term in sub_terms:\n                if self.grow_filter and term in args_map:\n                    continue\n                cloned_args = list(expr.args)\n                cloned_args.append(term)\n                args_sets.append(cloned_args)\n\n        for i, e in enumerate(expr.args):\n            if not e.is_Atom:\n                lim_sub = limit_sub or not (e.is_Add or e.is_Mul)\n                ee = self._add_extend(e, limit_sub=lim_sub)\n                if len(ee) > 0:\n                    args_map = set(expr.args)\n                    for vs in ee:\n                        if self.grow_filter and expr.is_Add and vs in args_map:\n                            continue\n                        cloned_args = list(expr.args)\n                        cloned_args[i] = vs\n                        args_sets.append(cloned_args)\n\n        for args in args_sets:\n            args = tuple(args)\n            tmp = expr.func(*args)\n            new_exprs.append(tmp)\n\n        return self._uniquify(new_exprs)\n\n    def _mul_extend(\n        self, expr, limit_sub: bool = False\n    ) -> list:\n        \"\"\"Multiplication extension — add factors to Mul nodes.\"\"\"\n        new_exprs: list = []\n\n        if expr.is_Atom:\n            return new_exprs\n\n        args_sets: list = []\n\n        if expr.is_Mul:\n            sub_terms = self.mul_extend_terms\n            if limit_sub:\n                sub_terms = self.mul_extend_lim_terms\n            for term in sub_terms:\n                cloned_args = list(expr.args)\n                cloned_args.append(term)\n                args_sets.append(cloned_args)\n\n        for i, e in enumerate(expr.args):\n            if not e.is_Atom:\n                lim_sub = limit_sub or not (e.is_Add or e.is_Mul)\n                ee = self._mul_extend(e, limit_sub=lim_sub)\n                if     continue\n                        cloned_args = list(expr.args)\n                        cloned_args[i] = vs\n                        args_sets.append(cloned_args)\n\n        for args in args_sets:\n            args = tuple(args)\n            tmp = expr.func(*args)\n            new_exprs.append(tmp)\n\n        return self._uniquify(new_exprs)\n\n    def _add_extend_top_level(self, expr) -> list:\n        \"\"\"Top-level addition extension (non-recursive).\"\"\"\n        if not expr.is_Add:\n            return []\n\n        new_terms: list = []\n        for e in expr.args:\n expr.is_Atom:\n            return []\n\n        new_exprs: list = []\n\n        if expr.is_Add:\n            for i, e in enumerate(expr.args):\n                cloned_args = list(expr.args)\n                del cloned_args[i]\n                smaller_add = expr.func(*cloned_args)\n                new_exprs.append(smaller_add)\n\n        args_sets: list = []\n        for i, e in pass_set = set()\n        for p in exprs:\n            s = p.evalf()\n            pass_set.add(s)\n        return list(pass_set)\n\n    def _toggle_plus_C(self, expr) -> sympy.Expr:\n        \"\"\"Add or remove a bare ``C`` from an addition.\"\"\"\n        if expr.is_Add:\n            hasC = any(e == C for e in expr.args)\n            if not hasC:\n                return expr + C\n            args = tuple(e for e in expr.args if e != C)\n            return expr.func(*args)\n        return sympy.Add(expr, C)\n",

    self.multi_expanders = []\n        for p in self.multi_expander_params:\n            funcs = map_names_to_funcs(p.get(\"usable_funcs\", [\"sin\", \"cos\", \"exp\", \"log\"]))\n            grow_params = p.get(\"grow_params\", {})\n            grower = Grower(self.vars, funcs, **grow_params)\n            self.multi_expanders.append(\n                {\n                    \"pop_count\": self._get_default_filters())\n\n        # Memoize\n        to_alge = []\n        if self.algebra_methods:\n            to_alge = self._memoize_models(to_memo)\n\n            # Algebra\n to_peek = to_alge + to_peek\n\n        # Evaluate\n        if self.peek_npts == 0:\n            to_eval = to_peek\n        else:\n            self._eval_models(to_peek, peek=True)\n     self._final_push(to_eval)\n        self.multi_expanders[0][\"nsga2_list\"].extend(to_eval)\n\n        self.curr_time = time.time()\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Main loop\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _loop(self, iterations: int) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Run the main search loop for *iterations* iterations.\"\"\"\n        for I in range(iterations):\n            self.curr_iter = I\n\n            # Multi-expand and grow\n            expanded = []\n            prev = []\n            for i, expander in enumerate(self.multi_expanders):\n                nsga2_list = expander[\"nsga2_list\"]\n                pop_count = expander[\"pop_count\"]\n                grower = expander[\"grower\"]\n\n                if prev:\n                    nsga2_list.extend(prev)\n                    prev = []\n\n                popped, nsga2_list = self._heap_pop(nsga2_list, pop_count)\n                expander[\"nsga2_list\"] = nsga2_list\n\n                # Grow each popped model\n                for p in popped:\n                    children = grower.grow(p)\n                    expanded.extend(children)\n\n            if not expanded:\n                continue\n\n            self._assign_iter_id(expanded)\n\n to_alge = self._memoize_models(to_memo)\n                algebrad = self._algebra_models(to_alge)\n                self._assign_iter_id(algebrad)\n                to_memo = filter_models(algebrad, self._get_default_filters())\n                to_memo = self._memoize_models(to_memo)\n\n            to_peek = self._memoize_models(to_memo)\n            to_peek = to_alge + to_peek\n\n            # Peek evaluate\n            if self.peek_npts == 0:\n                to_eval = to_peek\n            else:\n                self._eval_models(to_peek, peek=True)\n self._final_push(to_eval)\n                self.multi_expanders[0][\"nsga2_list\"].extend(to_eval)\n\n            self.curr_time = time.time()\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Evaluation helpers\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _eval_models(self, models: List[SearchModel], peek: bool = False) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Fit and evaluate a list of models.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        models:\n            Models to evaluate.\n        peek:\n            If ``True``, store results in peek attributes.\n        \"\"\"\n        for modl in models:\n            if modl.errored or modl.jax_model is None:\n                modl.errored = True\n                continue\n\n            try:\n                xs_inputs = [jnp.asarray(self.X_peek[:, i], dtype=jnp.float64) for i in range(self.X_peek.shape[1])]\n                y_true = jnp.asarray(self.Y_peek, dtype=jnp.float64)\n\n                fit_result = fit_model(modl.jax_model, y_true, *xs_inputs, max_iter=200)\n\n                if not fit_result.success:\n                    modl.errored = True\n                    continue\n\n                # Store fitted coefficients\n                modl.jax_model.c_values = fit_result.coefficients\n\n                # Evaluate on full data for score\n                full_xs = [jnp.asarray(self.X_train[:, i], dtype=jnp.float64) for i in range(self.X_train.shape[1])]\n                full_y = jnp.asarray(self.Y_train, dtype=jnp.float64)\n                y_pred = modl.jax_model.jax_fun(fit_result.coefficients, *full_xs)\n\n                eval_result = evaluate(modl.jax_model, full_y, y_pred)\n\n                # Update model with results\n                modl.score = eval_result.score\n                modl.r2 = eval_result.r2\n                modl.evar = eval_result.evar\n                modl.aic = eval_result.aic\n                modl.bic = eval_result.bic\n                modl.chisqr = eval_result.chisqr\n                modl.redchi = eval_result.redchi\n                modl.mae = eval_result.mae\n                modl.rmae = eval_result.rmae\n                modl.eval_nfev += fit_result.nfev\n\n                if peek:\n                    modl.peek_score = modl.peek_bic = eval_result.bic\n                    modl.peek_redchi = eval_result.redchi\n                    modl.peek_nfev = fit_result.nfev\n                    self.peek_nfev += modl.peek_nfev\n                    self.peekd_models += 1\n                    modl.peeked = True\n                else:\n                    self.eval_nfev += modl.eval_nfev\n                    self.evald_models += 1\n                    modl.evaluated = True\n\n                # Track parent improvement\n                self._compute_improvements(modl)\n\n            except Exception:\n                modl.errored = True\n\n    def _compute_improvements(self, modl: SearchModel) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Compute improvement over parent model.\"\"\"\n        if modl.parent_id >= 0 and modl.parent_id < len(self.models):\n            parent = self.models[modl.parent_id]\n            if parent.score is not None:\n                modl.improve_score = parent.score - modl.score\n            if parent.r2 is not None:\n                modl.improve_r2 = modl.r2 - parent.r2\n            if parent.evar is not None:\n                modl.improve_evar = modl.evar - parent.evar\n            if parent.aic is not None:\n                modl.improve_aic = parent.aic - modl.aic\n            if parent.bic is not None:\n                modl.improve_bic = parent.bic - modl.bic\n            if parent.redchi is not None:\n                modl.improve_redchi = parent.redchi - modl.redchi\n        else:\n            # First generation — small negative improvement\n            if modl.score is not None:\n                modl.improve_score = -0.000001 * modl.score\n            if modl.r2 is not None:\n                modl.improve_r2 = -0.000001 * modl.r2\n            if modl.evar is not None:\n                modl.improve_evar = -0.000001 * modl.evar\n            if modl.aic is not None:\n                modl.improve_aic = -0.000001 * modl.aic\n            if modl.bic is not None:\n                modl.improve_bic = -0.000001 * modl.bic\n            if modl.redchi is not None:\n                modl.improve_redchi = -0.000001 * modl.redchi\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Heap operations\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _peek_push_models(self, models: List[SearchModel]) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Push peek-evaluated models to the peek heap.\"\"\"\n        ms = [m for m in models if m is not None and not m.errored and m.score is not None]\n        self.nsga2_peek.extend(ms)\n        for m in ms:\n            m.peek_queued = True\n\n    def _peek_pop(self) -> List[SearchModel]:\n        \"\"\"Pop best models from the peek heap for full evaluation.\"\"\"\n        popped, self.nsga2_peek = self._heap_pop(self.nsga2_peek, self.peek_count)\n        for p in popped:\n            p.peek_popped = True\n        return popped\n\n    def _final_push(self, models: List[SearchModel]) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Push fully evaluated models to the final list.\"\"\"\n        ms = [m for m in models if m is not None and not m.errored and m.score is not None]\n        for p in ms:\n            self.final.append(p)\n            p.finalized = True\n\n    def _heap_pop(\n        self, heap_list: List[SearchModel], pop_count: int\n    ) -> Tuple[List[SearchModel], List[SearchModel]]:\n        \"\"\"Select *pop_count* best models from *heap_list* via NSGA-II.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        tuple[list, list]\n            ``(popped, remaining)``.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Set fitness values\n        self._compute_fitness(heap_list)\n\n        popped = selNSGA2(heap_list, pop_count, nd=\"log\")\n\n        remaining = [m for m in heap_list if m not in popped]\n\n        return popped, remaining\n\n    def _compute_fitness(self, models: List[SearchModel]) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Compute fitness values for a list of models.\n\n        Uses the configured fitness function parameters.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Build fitness calculator on first call\n        if self.fitness_calc is None and models:\n            from pge_jax.fitness_funcs import build_fitness_calc\n\n            self.fitness_calc = build_fitness_calc(self.fitness_func_params)\n\n        if self.fitness_calc is not None:\n            self.fitness_calc(models)\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Filtering, memoization, algebra\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _get_default_filters(self) -> list:\n        \"\"\"Return the default filter list with configured max_size.\"\"\"\n        from pge_jax.filters import (\n            filter_just_C,\n            filter_has_big_pow,\n            filter_has_coeff_pow,\n            filter_has_int_coeff,\n            filter_no_C,\n            filter_too_big,\n        )\n\n        return [\n            lambda m, e: filter_too_big(m, e, big=self.max_size),\n            filter_has_int_coeff,\n            lambda m, e: filter_has_big_pow(m, e, big=self.max_power),\n            filter_just_C,\n            filter_no_C,\n            filter_has_coeff_pow,\n        ]\n\n    def _memoize_models(self, models: List[SearchModel]) -> List[SearchModel]:\n        \"\"\"Deduplicate models and assign IDs.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        list[SearchModel]\n            Only newly inserted (unique) models.\n        \"\"\"\n        unique = []\n        for m in models:\n            h = m.orig.__hash__()\n            r = self.hmap.get(h, None)\n            if r is None:\n                m.id = len(self.models)\n                self.models.append(m)\n                self.hmap[h] = m\n                m.memoized = True\n                unique.append(m)\n        return unique\n\n    def _algebra_models(\n        self, models: List[SearchModel]\n    ) -> List[SearchModel]:\n        \"\"\"Apply algebraic manipulation to models.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        list[SearchModel]\n            New models whose expressions changed.\n        \"\"\"\n        alges: List[SearchModel] = []\n        for modl in models:\n            for meth in self.algebra_methods:\n                try:\n                    manipd, err = manip_model(modl, meth)\n                    if err is not None:\n                        if err == \"same\":\n                            continue\n                        continue\n                    if manipd is not None:\n                        manipd.parent_id = modl.id\n                        manipd.gen_relation = meth\n                        alges.append(manipd)\n                except Exception:\n                    continue\n            modl.algebrad = True\n        return alges\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Utilities\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _assign_iter_id(self, expr_list: List[SearchModel]) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Set ``iter_id`` for a list of models.\"\"\"\n        for e in expr_list:\n            e.iter_id = self.curr_iter\n\n    def print_best(self, count: int = 16) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Print the best models from the final list.\"\"\"\n        if not self.final:\n            print(\"No models evaluated yet.\")\n            return\n\n        # Compute fitness\n        self._compute_fitness(self.final)\n\n        # Sort into Pareto fronts\n        fronts = sortLogNondominated(self.final, count)\n\n        print(f\"Best {min(count, len(self.final))} of {len(self.final)}\")\n        print(\"-\" * 100)\n\n        cnt = 0\n        for front in fronts:\n            for m in front:\n                if cnt >= count:\n                    break\n                cnt += 1\n                m.pretty_expr()\n                print(f\"  {m}\")\n            if cnt >= count:\n                break\n\n        print(\"-\" * 100)\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Finalize\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def finalize(self, nfronts: int = 4) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Generate final Pareto fronts and print results.\"\"\"\n        print(\"\\nFinalizing\\n\")\n\n        # Combine final + remaining population\n        final = self.final + [\n            m for exp in self.multi_expanders for m in exp[\"nsga2_list\"]\n        ]\n\n        # Compute fitness\n        self._compute_fitness(final)\n\n        # Generate Pareto fronts\n        self.final_paretos = sortLogNondominated(final, len(final))\n\n        # Print results\n        print(\"Final Results\")\n        if self.final_paretos:\n            print(self.final_paretos[0][0].print_columns() if hasattr(self.final_paretos[0][0], 'print_columns') else str(self.final_paretos[0][0]))\n            print(\"-\" * 100)\n            for i, front in enumerate(self.final_paretos[:nfronts]):\n                for m in front:\n                    print(f\"  {m}\")\n                print(\"\")\n\n        print(f\"\\nnum peekd models:  {self.peekd_models}\")\n        print(f\"num evald models:  {self.evald_models}\")\n        print(f\"num peek evals:    {self.peek_nfev} ({self.peek_nfev * self.peek_npts} point-evals)\")\n        print(f\"num eval evals:    {self.eval_nfev} ({self.eval_nfev * self.eval_npts} point-evals)\")\n        print(f\"num total evals:   {self.peek_nfev * self.peek_npts + self.eval_nfev * self.eval_npts}\")\n\n        runtime = time.time() - self.start_time\n        print(f\"TOTAL RUN TIME: {runtime:.4f} seconds\")\n\n    def get_final_paretos(self) -> Optional[List[List[SearchModel]]]:\n        \"\"\"Return the final Pareto fronts.\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        list[list[SearchModel]] | None\n            List of Pareto fronts, or ``None`` if not yet finalised.\n        \"\"\"\n        return self.final_paretos\n\n    def get_best_model(self) -> Optional[SearchModel]:\n        \"\"\"Return the single best model (lowest RMSE on the first Pareto front).\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        SearchModel | None\n        \"\"\"\n        if not self.final_paretos or not self.final_paretos[0]:\n pge_jax.filters import (\n    default_filters,\n    filter_has_big_pow,\n    filter_has_coeff_pow,\n    filter_has_int_coeff,\n    filter_just_C,\n    filter_model,\n    filter_models,\n isDominated,\n    selNSGA2,\n    selSPEA2,\n    sortLogNondominated,\n    sortNondominated,\n)\nfrom pge_jax.fitness_funcs import (\n    build_fitness_calc,\n    build_fitness_weights,\n    build_value_extractor,\n)\nfrom pge_jax.expand import Grower, map_names_to_funcs\n\n\nclass TestSearchModel:\n\n    def test_init_basic(self):\n        x = sympy.Symbol(\"x\")\n        C1 = sympy.Symbol(\"C_0\")\n        expr = C1 * x + 1\n        m = SearchModel(expr, xs=[x], cs=[C1])\n        assert m.inited is True\n        assert m.id == -2\n        assert m.parent_id == -2\n        assert m.gen_relation == \"unknown\"\n        assert m.xs == [x]\n        assert m.cs == [C1]\n\n    def test_rewrite_coeff(self):\n        C = sympy.Symbol(\"C\")\n        x = sympy.Symbol(\"x\")\n        expr = C * x + C + 1\n        m = SearchModel(expr, xs=[x])\n        m.rewrite_coeff()\n        assert len(m.cs) == 2\n        assert sympy.Symbol(\"C_0\") in m.cs\n        assert sympy.Symbol(\"C_1\") in m.cs\n        assert m.jax_model is not None\n\n    def test_calc_tree_size(self):\n        x = sympy.Symbol(\"x\")\n        expr = x ** 2 + 1\n        m = SearchModel(expr)\n        sz, psz = m.calc_tree_size()\n        assert sz > 0\n        assert psz >= sz\n\n    def test_dominates(self):\n        m1 = SearchModel(sympy.Symbol(\"C_0\") * sympy.Symbol(\"x\"))\n        m2 ## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-MTP (coding) · 33.3s)

_Thinking:_

The issue is that `filter_just_C` compares against `C` from the filters module, but the test creates a different `C` symbol. The filter compares `modl.orig == C` where `C` is from the filters module. Let me check the filter code and fix the test to match.

Actually, looking more carefully at the filter code:
```python
def filter_just_C(modl: SearchModel, expr) -> bool:
    if modl.orig is C or modl.orig == C or modl.orig.is_Number:
        return True
    return False
```

It checks `modl.orig == C` where `C` is `sympy.Symbol("C")` from the filters module. So if I create `C = sympy.Symbol("C")` in the test, the equality should work. Let me check the `_make_model` method.

The `_make_model` calls `m.rewrite_coeff()` which replaces bare `C` with `C_0, C_1, ...`. So after `rewrite_coeff()`, `modl.orig` is no longer `C` — it's been rewritten. The filter checks `modl.orig`, which has been rewritten.

So the test needs to check `modl.orig` BEFORE rewrite, or the filter needs to be updated. Let me look at how pypge does it - it checks `modl.orig` which is the original expression before rewrite.

Actually, looking at the original pypge code:
```python
def filter_just_C(modl,expr):
    if modl.orig is C or modl.orig == C or modl.orig.is_Number:
        return True
    return False
```

And in `filter_model`:
```python
def filter_model(modl, expr, filters):
    for e in preorder_traversal(expr):
```


So the filter receives `modl.orig` as the expression to check. In pypge, `modl.orig` is the original expression before coefficient rewriting, and `modl.expr` is the expanded version. In my SearchModel, `self.orig` is set to the original expression and `self.expr` is `sympy.expand(expr)`, but `rewrite_coeff()` modifies `self.expr` while preserving the original.

Looking at the pypge implementation, `rewrite_coeff()` actually changes `self.expr` to the rewritten version and updates `self.cs` accordingly, while `self.orig` gets transformed into a form where bare `C` symbols are replaced with the `CS` array. The filter checks `modl.orig` which contains the modified expression after this transformation.

In my SearchModel, `rewrite_coeff()` is creating `self.cs` from scratch rather than using the provided `cs` list, and it's setting `self.expr` to the rewritten expression. The key difference is that pypge stores the rewritten expression in `self.expr`, not in `self.orig`.

Looking at the filter logic, it checks `modl.orig` which should be the original expression before coefficient rewriting. The test is failing because after calling `rewrite_coeff()`, the `C` symbol in the expression gets replaced with `C_0`, so the filter no longer finds it. I need to either check the original expression before rewriting or adjust how the filter accesses the expression.

The pypge approach uses `modl.orig` to check the expression after `rewrite_coeff()` has already been called, which means the coefficient symbols have already been transformed. I should follow the same pattern rather than trying to check before the transformation happens.

    def sortLogNondominated(
        individuals: List[Any],
        k: int,
        first_front_only: bool = False,
    ) -> List[List[Any]]:
        """Generalized Reduced Run-Time Complexity Non-Dominated Sorting.
    
        Uses the algorithm of Fortin et al. (2013).
    
        Parameters
        ----------
        individuals:
            List of individuals (must have ``wvalues`` attribute).
        k:
            Number of individuals to sort.
        first_front_only:
            If ``True``, return only the first front.
    
        Returns

        list[list]
            List of Pareto fronts.

            return []

        for i, ind in enumerate(individuals):
            unique_fits[ind.wvalues].append(ind)

        fitnesses = list(unique_fits.keys())
        front = dict.fromkeys(fitnesses, 0)

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-MTP (coding) · 9.5s)

_Thinking:_

Interesting - the semantics are reversed from what I expected. Let me check the code:

```python
def isDominated(wvalues1, wvalues2):
    not_equal = False
    for self_w, other_w in zip(wvalues1, wvalues2):
        if self_w > other_w:
            return False
        if self_w < other_w:
            not_equal = True
    return not_equal
```

So `isDominated(A, B)` returns True if A is dominated by B. It checks if all values in A are >= corresponding values in B, with at least one strictly greater.

So `isDominated((1,2), (2,3))` returns True because 1<2 and 2<3, so (1,2) is better than (2,3). This means (1,2) is NOT dominated by (2,3) — actually wait, the function says "returns True if wvalues1 is dominated by wvalues2".

Let me re-read: "Returns: True if wvalues2 dominates wvalues1". So `isDominated((1,2), (2,3))` returns True means (2,3) dominates (1,2). But that's wrong for minimization!

Actually, looking at the docstring: "Minimization semantics: lower is better." So if (1,2) is better than (2,3), then (1,2) dominates (2,3), not the other way

```
def isDominated(wvalues1, wvalues2):
    """Returns whether or not *wvalues1* dominates *wvalues2*.
    
    :param wvalues1: The weighted fitness values that would be dominated.
    :param wvalues2: The weighted fitness values of the dominant.
    :returns: :obj:`True` if wvalues2 dominates wvalues1, :obj:`False`
              otherwise.
    """
    not_equal = False
    for self_wvalue, other_wvalue in zip(wvalues1, wvalues2):
        if self_wvalue > other_wvalue:
            return False
        elif self_wvalue < other_wvalue:
            not_equal = True
    return not_equal

def median(seq, key=identity):
    """Returns the median of *seq* - the numeric value separating the higher 
    half of a sample from the lower half. If there is an even number of 
    elements in *seq*, it returns the mean of the two middle values.
    """

```

## Assistant (Build · Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-MTP (coding) · 38.8s)

_Thinking:_

OK so the docstring says "Returns whether or not wvalues1 dominates wvalues2" but then the description says "wvalues1: The weighted fitness values that would be dominated" and "returns True if wvalues2 dominates wvalues1". So the function returns True if wvalues2 dominates wvalues1 (i.e., wvalues1 is dominated by wvalues2).

For minimization semantics with the fitness weights applied:
- Negative weights mean minimize (lower is better)
- Positive weights mean maximize (higher is better)

So the function is comparing weighted fitness values. If wvalues2 dominates wvalues1, it means wvalues2 is better in all objectives.

For example, with minimization objectives where lower is better:
- wvalues1 = (2.0, 3.0), wvalues2 = (1.0, 2.0)
- wvalues2 is better in both dimensions (1 < 2 and 2 < 3)
- So wvalues2 dominates wvalues1, and isDominated should return True

But the code does:
```python
for self_wvalue, other_wvalue in zip(wvalues1, wvalues2):
    if self_wvalue > other_wvalue:  # 2 > 1 -> True
        return False
```

This returns False, which means "wvalues1 is NOT dominated by wvalues2" when it clearly should be.

Wait, I need to think about this more carefully. The fitness weights are applied:
- Negative weight = minimize (lower is better)
- Positive weight = maximize (higher is better)

So after applying weights, the comparison is: lower weighted value is always better.

If we have objectives like `["-(1)jpsz", "-score", "+r2"]`:
- jpsz: weight -1, so lower jpsz -> higher weighted value (more negative) -> better
- score: weight -1, so lower score -> higher weighted value (more negative) -> better
- r2: weight +1, so higher r2 -> higher weighted value -> better

Wait, that doesn't work either. Let me think again...

Actually, the fitness values are set as `wvals = tuple(w * v for w, v in zip(weights, vals))`. So:
- For jpsz=10, weight=-1: weighted value = -10
- For score=0.5, weight=-1: weighted value = -0.5
- For r2=0.9, weight=+1: weighted value = 0.9

And the comparison is: higher weighted value is better (because we want to maximize the weighted fitness).

So isDominated checks: does wvalues2 dominate wvalues1? Meaning, is wvalues2 >= wvalues1 in all objectives and strictly > in at least one?

The code:
```python
for self_wvalue, other_wvalue in zip(wvalues1, wvalues2):
    if self_wvalue > other_wvalue:  # wvalues1 > wvalues2 -> wvalues1 is better -> not dominated
        return False
    elif self_wvalue < other_wvalue:  # wvalues1 < wvalues2 -> wvalues2 is better
        not_equal = True
return not_equal
```

So isDominated((2.0, 3.0), (1.0, 2.0)):
- self=2, other=1: 2 > 1 -> return False (wvalues1 is better in this dim, so not dominated)

This is correct for MAXIMIZATION semantics. In the PGE context, the weighted fitness values are constructed so that higher is better (because negative weights flip minimization objectives to maximization).

So the test was wrong. Let me fix it.

isDominated((2.0, 3.0), (1.0, 2.0)) = False means: (2,3) is NOT dominated by (1,2) in maximization terms. Since 2 > 1 and 3 > 2, (2,3) is BETTER than (1,2) in maximization terms. So (1,2) is dominated by (2,3), not the other way around.

In the PGE context with weights like `["-(1)jpsz", "-score"]`:
- Model A: jpsz=10, score=0.5 -> weighted = (-10, -0.5)
- Model B: jpsz=5, score=0.3 -> weighted = (-5, -0.3)
- -5 > -10 and -0.3 > -0.5, so B is better in both dimensions
- isDominated((-10, -0.5), (-5, -0.3)) = True because (-10) < (-5) and (-0.5) < (-0.3)

So the test assertion was wrong. Let me fix it.


The test had wrong assertions — `isDominated` uses maximization semantics (higher weighted value is better, which is achieved by negating minimization objectives). Let me fix it.
